**naivānyadā lauham ivāprataptaṁ**

**sthāneṣu tad draṣṭr-apadeśam eti ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **teṣāṁ tad-ajñāne hetum āha—**dehendriyādayo’mī** **yad-aṁśa-viddhā** yac-caitanyāṁśenāviṣṭāḥ santaḥ **karmasu** sva-sva-viṣayeṣu **pracaranti** jāgrat-svapnayoḥ | **anyadā** suṣupti-mūrcchādau naiva pracaranti, yathā **aprataptaṁ lohaṁ** na dahati | ato yathā lauham agni-śaktyaiva dāhakaṁ sad, agniṁ vinā na dahati, evaṁ brahma-gata-jñāna-kriyā-śaktibhyāṁ pravartamānā dehādayas tan na spṛśanti na viduś ceti bhāvaḥ | 

jīvas tarhi draṣṭṛtvāj jānātu ? nety āha—**sthāneṣu** jāgrad-ādiṣu **draṣṭr-apadeśaṁ** draṣṭṛ-saṁjñāṁ tad eva **eti** prāpnoti, nānyo jīvo nāmāsti, nānyo’to’sti draṣṭā [bṛ.ā.u. 3.7.23] ity-ādi-śruteḥ | yad vā, **draṣṭr-apadeśaṁ** draṣṭṛ-saṁjñaṁ jīvam api tad evaiti jānāti, na tu jīvas taj jānātīty arthaḥ | tad uktaṁ haṁsa-guhya-stotre deho’savo’kṣā[^19] [bhā.pu. 6.4.25] ity-ādi ||24||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **dehendriya iti | atrādvaita-śārīrake’pi sāṅkhyam ākṣipyoktaṁ, yathā, atha punaḥ sākṣi-nimittam īkṣitṛtvaṁ pradhānasya kalpyeta yathāgni-nimittam ayaḥ-piṇḍāder dagdhṛtvaṁ, tathā sati yan-nimittam īkṣitatṛtvaṁ pradhānasya, tad eva sarvajñaṁ mukhyaṁ jagataḥ kāraṇam [śaṅkara-bhāṣya, 1.1.5] iti |

śrutiś cātra—tam eva bhāntam anubhāti [kaṭha.u. 2.2.15], ko hy evānyāt kaḥ prāṇyāt yad eṣa ākāśa ānando na syāt [tai.u. 2.7], cakṣuṣaś cakṣur uta śrotrasya śrotram [bṛ.ā.u. 4.4.18] ity-ādyā ṭīkotthāpita-śrutau[^20] ca, jīvo nāmato nānyaḥ svayaṁ-siddho nāsti, parantu tad-ātmaka evety arthaḥ | tathāto’nyo draṣṭā nāsti, sarva-draṣṭus tasyāparo draṣṭā nāstīty arthaḥ iti vyākhyeyam ||24|| [bhagavat-sandarbha 15]

**dehendriya-prāṇa-mano-dhiyo’mī**

**yad-aṁśa-viddhāḥ pracaranti karmasu |**

**naivānyadā lauham ivāprataptaṁ**

**sthāneṣu tad draṣṭr-apadeśam eti ||**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **teṣāṁ tad-ajñāne hetum āha—dehendriyeti | **yad-aṁśa-viddhāḥ** yac caitanyāṁśenāviṣṭāḥ santaḥ **karmasu** sva-sva-viṣayeṣu **caranti **jāgrat-svapnayoḥ, **anyadā** suṣuptiḥ mūrcchādau **naiva** pracaranti | yad vā, **aprataptaṁ lauhaṁ **na dahati | ato yathā lauham agni-śaktyaiva dāhakaṁ sad agniṁ na dahati, evam eva brahma-śaktyaiva sva-sva-viṣayeṣu pravartamānā dehādayo brahma na spṛśanti, nāpi jānantīti bhāvaḥ | 

jīvas tarhi draṣṭṛtvāj jānātu ? tatrāha—**sthāneṣu** jāgrad-ādiṣu **draṣṭr-apadeśaṁ** draṣṭṛ-saṁjñaṁ jīvam api karma-bhūtaṁ tad brahmaiva kartṛ **eti** jīvasya draṣṭṛtva-siddhy-arthaṁ, svīya-kiñcic-caitanya-prāpaṇena svayam eva taṁ prāpnotīty arthaḥ | mama ādāya iva jīvā api jaḍā iti ca ke’py ācakṣate | yad vā, tad brahmaiva tam eti jānāti, na tu jīvo brahma jānātīty arthaḥ | yad uktaṁ haṁsa-guhya-stave—deho’savo’kṣā [bhā.pu. 6.4.25] ity-ādi ||24||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.25 ||**

**oṁ namo bhagavate mahā-puruṣāya mahānubhāvāya mahā-vibhūti-pataye sakala-sātvata-parivṛḍha-nikara-kara-kamala-kuḍmalopalālita-caraṇāravinda-yugala parama-parameṣṭhin namas te.**

**śrīdharaḥ : sakalā** ye **sātvata-parivṛḍhāḥ,** teṣāṁ **nikaraḥ** samūhaḥ, tasya **kara-kamalānāṁ kuḍmalair** mukulair **upalālitaṁ caraṇāravinda-yugalaṁ** yasya, tasya saṁbodhanam | **param** utkṛṣṭa | **parameṣṭhin** sarveśvara ||25||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **sākṣād-bhagavattvena stauti—oṁ nama iti | tad evaṁ saṅkarṣaṇopāsanāpi dvāram eva | tasya sātvata-śāstra-vigrahatvena [6.16.33] vakṣyamāṇatvāt **paramaṁ** phalaṁ tu śrī-bhagavān ity abhipretam ||25||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mahā-mantrasya jñāna-prakāśakatvam uktvā bhakti-rasa-paripūrṇatvam āha—om iti | **sakala-sātvata-parivṛḍhāḥ** sarva-bhakta-śreṣṭhāḥ, teṣāṁ **nikarasya** **kara-kamalānāṁ kuṭmalena upalālitaṁ** laghu laghu saṁvāhana-vaidagdhyā prīṇitaṁ **caraṇāravinda-yugalaṁ** yasya, he tathābhūteti mām api sva-pāda-saṁvāhana-sevāyāṁ sthāpayety abhilāṣo dhvanitaḥ | 

nanu tvām atinikṛṣṭaṁ tasyām atyutkṛṣṭa-sevāyāṁ kathaṁ niyuñje ? ity ata āha—he **parama parameṣṭhin**, parama parameśvara kartum anyathā-kartuṁ ca samarthaḥ ||25||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.26 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**bhaktāyaitāṁ prapannāya vidyām ādiśya nāradaḥ |**

**yayāv aṅgirasā sākaṁ dhāma svāyambhuvaṁ prabho ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrve sa-nārado’ṅgirā ājagāmety aṅgirāḥ prādhānyenoktaḥ | citraketoḥ putra-pradatvena tasya pṛthag-uktatvāt | iha tu **nārado**’**ṅgirasā sākaṁ yayāv** iti nāradasya prādhānya-nirdeśaḥ | tad-upadeśena tasya vairāgyotpatteḥ | **prabho** ! he samartha ! ||26||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **etām ity aneka-vākya-garbhām ekām eva vidyāṁ mahatīm | atra citraketave putra-pradatvenāṅgirasaḥ prādhānyaṁ, mantra-pradatvena tu nāradasya | ata eva pūrvam aṅgirāḥ sa-nārada ājagāmety uktaṁ, samprati **yayāv aṅgirasā** **nārada** ity ucyate | he **prabho** ! etad-ādy-abhiprāya-jñāne parama-samartha ! ||26||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.27 ||**

**citraketus tu tāṁ vidyāṁ yathā nārada-bhāṣitām |**

**dhārayām āsa saptāham ab-bhakṣaḥ susamāhitaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yathā yathāvad dhārayām āsa ||27||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.28 ||**

**tataḥ sa sapta-rātrānte vidyayā dhāryamāṇayā |**

**vidyādharādhipatyaṁ ca lebhe’pratihataṁ nṛpa ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : vidyādharādhipatyaṁ** cāvāntara-phalaṁ **lebhe** | **apratihatam** askhalitam ||28||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **prathamam avāntara-phalam āha—**vidyādharādhipatyam** iti ||28||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.29 ||**

**tataḥ katipayāhobhir vidyayeddha-mano-gatiḥ |**

**jagāma deva-devasya śeṣasya caraṇāntikam ||**

**madhvaḥ : **anyāntaryāminaṁ viṣṇum upāsyānya-samīpagaḥ |


    bhaved yogyatayā tasya padaṁ vā prāpnuyān naraḥ || iti nāradīye |

anena prakāreṇa muhus tat-sakāśam abhyagāt | 


    śeṣāntaryāminaṁ viṣṇuṁ citraketur upāsyatu |


    śeṣāviṣṭa-hareś cāpi varān prāpyapatad gatim || iti tantra-mālāyām ||29||

**śrīdharaḥ : katipayair ahobhiḥ** | **vidyayeddhena** dīptena **manasā gatir** yasya ||29||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mukhyaṁ phalam āha—jagāmeti ||29||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.30 ||**

**mṛṇāla-gauraṁ śiti-vāsasaṁ sphurat-**

**kirīṭa-keyūra-kaṭitra-kaṅkaṇam |**

**prasanna-vaktrāruṇa-locanaṁ vṛtaṁ**

**dadarśa siddheśvara-maṇḍalaiḥ prabhum ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : mṛṇālavad gauram** | **śiti-vāsasaṁ** nīlāmbaram | **sphuranti kirīṭādīni** yasya | **kaṭitraṁ** kaṭi-sūtram | **prasannāni** **vaktrāṇi** yasya | **aruṇāni locanāni** yasya taṁ ca taṁ ca ||30||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : siti-vāsasaṁ** nīlāmbaraṁ, **kaṭitraṁ** kaṭi-sūtram ||30||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.31 ||**

**tad-darśana-dhvasta-samasta-kilbiṣaḥ**

**svasthāmalāntaḥkaraṇo’bhyayān muniḥ |**

**pravṛddha-bhaktyā praṇayāśru-locanaḥ**

**prahṛṣṭa-romānamad ādi-puruṣam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **dṛṣṭvā ca tam **ādi-pūruṣam abhyayāc** charaṇaṁ gataḥ | **anaman** nanāma | kathaṁ-bhūtaḥ ? tasya **darśanena dhvastaṁ samastaṁ kilbiṣaṁ** yasya | **svaccham amalaṁ cāntaḥ-karaṇaṁ** yasya | **praṇayenāśru**-mukte **locane** yasya | **prahṛṣṭāni romāṇi** yasya saḥ ||31||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tad-darśaneti | kilbiṣa-mātraṁ bhagavat-prāpty-asaṁbhāvanā-mayaṁ duḥkhaṁ jñeyam | dṛṣṭvā ca abhyayāt abhimukham agacchat | abhyetya cānamat ||31||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.32 ||**

**sa uttamaśloka-padābja-viṣṭaraṁ**

**premāśru-leśair upamehayan muhuḥ |**

**premoparuddhākhila-varṇa-nirgamo**

**naivāśakat taṁ prasamīḍituṁ ciram ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **taṁ **prasamīḍituṁ** stotuṁ **ciraṁ** **naivāśakan** na śaśāka | tatra hetuḥ—**uttama-ślokasya pādābjayor viṣṭaram** āsanam **upamehayann** abhiṣiñcan | **premṇoparuddho’khilānāṁ varṇānāṁ** **nirgama** uccāraṇaṁ yasya saḥ ||32||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **natvā tuṣṭāvety āha—sa iti | **viṣṭaraṁ** mānasaṁ, **upamehayan** abhiṣiñcan ||32||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.33 ||**

**tataḥ samādhāya mano manīṣayā**

**babhāṣa etat pratilabdha-vāg asau |**

**niyamya sarvendriya-bāhya-vartanaṁ**

**jagad-guruṁ sātvata-śāstra-vigraham ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : manīṣayā** buddhyā **manaḥ samādhāyaitad** vakṣyamāṇaṁ **babhāṣe** | **pratilabdhā vāk** yena | **sātvata-śāstrokto vigraho** yasya tam ||33||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : pratilabdha-vāk** tat-kṛpayaivety arthaḥ | **sātvata-śāstrokto vigraho** deho yasyety anena jñāna-śāstroktasya māyā-maya-vigrahatvasya prāmāṇyaṁ vāritam ||33||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.34 ||**

**citraketur uvāca—**

**ajita jitaḥ sama-matibhiḥ**

**sādhubhir bhavān jitātmabhir bhavatā |**

**vijitās te’pi ca bhajatām**

**akāmātmanāṁ ya ātmado’tikaruṇaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **

anyonya-premajānanda-nibhṛtān svāmi-sevakān |

abhinandan mudā stauti daśabhiḥ pañcabhir vibhum ||

he **ajita** ! anyair ajito’pi bhavān sādhubhir bhaktair **jitaḥ** svādhīna eva kṛtaḥ | yato **bhavān** **atikaruṇaḥ** | te’pi ca niṣkāmā api **bhavatā vijitāḥ** | yo bhavān **akāmātmanām ātmānam** eva **dadāti** ||34||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **hari-bhakti-sudhodaye ca prahlādaṁ prati śrī-mukha-vākyam—


    sa-bhayaṁ sambhramaṁ vatsa mad-gaurava-kṛtaṁ tyaja |


    naiṣa priyo me bhakteṣu svādhīna-praṇayī bhava ||


    api me pūrṇa-kāmasya navaṁ navam idaṁ priyam |


    niḥśaṅka-praṇayād bhakto yan māṁ paśyati bhāṣate ||


    sadā mukto’pi baddho’smi bhakteṣu sneha-rajjubhiḥ |


    ajito’pi jito’haṁ tair avaśyo’pi vaśīkṛtaḥ ||


    tyakta-bandhu-jana-sneho mayi yaḥ kurute ratim |


    ekas tasyāsmi sa ca me na cānyo’sty āvayoḥ suhṛt || [ha.bha.su. 14.27-30] iti |

tasmāt sādhu vyākhyātaṁ bhagavat-pratīti-rūpā vṛttir māyādimayī na bhavati | kiṁ tarhi svarūpa-śakty-ānanda-rūpā yadānanda-parādhīnaḥ śrī-bhagavān apīti | yathā ca śrīmatī gopālottara-tāpanī śrutiḥ—vijñāna-ghana ānanda-ghanaḥ sac-cid-ānandaika-rase bhakti-yoge tiṣṭhati [go.tā.u. 2.79] iti ||34|| [prīti-sandarbhaḥ 66]

**viśvanāthaḥ : **paraspara-vaśī-bhāva-labhyānanda-rasāmbudhau, majjetāṁ bhagavad-bhaktau bhaktyaivety āha saṁstuvan—he **ajita** ! jñāni-yogi-prabhṛtibhis tvam ajita eva, **sādhubhir** bhaktais tu **bhavān jitaḥ** adhīnīkṛtaḥ **sama-matibhiḥ** svakīya-sukha-duḥkha-sama-buddhibhir **jitātmabhir** jita-manaskatvena mano-dharmasya kāmasyāpi jitatvāt niṣkāmaiḥ teṣāṁ tad-upāsane niṣkāmatvam eva tvaj-jaye kāraṇam iti bhāvaḥ | 

**te sādhavo’pi bhavatā vijitāḥ**, yato **bhajatām akāmātmanāṁ** bhajadbhyo niṣkāmebhyaḥ yo **bhavān ātmadaḥ** ātmānam eva dadāti | yadi yūyaṁ māṁ paricarya kim apy apavargādikam api matto naiva vṛṇudhve, tarhi yatheṣṭaṁ rātrindinaṁ mām eva paricaratha mām ṛṇīkuruthety ātmānaṁ tebhyo dadad eva balād ātmanaḥ saundarya-sausvarya-saurabhyādīni tan-nayana-caraṇāravindādīndriya-bhogārtham arpayatīty arthaḥ | tena tad-vijaye bhavato’py ātmadatvam eva kāraṇam iti bhāvaḥ | 

atra sādhubhir iti jñānibhir apīti na vyākhyeyam | uttarārdhe **bhajatām akāmātmanām** iti viśeṣaṇa-dvayasya tad-vyavartakatvāt, jñānināṁ bhajanaṁ tu mokṣa-siddhy-arthaṁ sādhana-daśāyām eva | atra tu bhajatām iti vartamāna-nirdeśaḥ | niṣkāmatvaṁ tv ātyantika-duḥkha-nivṛtti-kāmatvāt teṣāṁ nāsty eva ||34||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.35 ||**

**tava vibhavaḥ khalu bhagavan**

**jagad-udaya-sthiti-layādīni |**

**viśva-sṛjas te’ṁśāṁśās tatra**

**mṛṣā spardhanti pṛthag abhimatyā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu bhaktair eva jita iti katham ? spardhamānair api sṛṣṭy-ādi-kartṛbhir anyair īśvarair jaya-sambhavāt tatrāha—taveti | **jagata udayādīni** **tavaiva vibhavo** vibhavanaṁ mahimā līleti yāvat | **ādi**-śabdena praveśa-niyamanādīni | **viśva-sṛjas** tu brahmādayo neśvarāḥ kintu **te tavāṁśo** yaḥ puruṣas **tasyāṁśāḥ** | **tatra** evaṁ-sthite’pi "pṛthak **pṛthag** īśvarā vayam" ity **abhimānena** vṛthaiva **spardhante** ||35||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : viśva-sṛjaḥ** brahma-rudrendrādyāḥ **aṁśāṁśāḥ** atyalpāṁśā ity arthaḥ ||35||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **evaṁ prabhu-bhaktayoḥ paraspara-vaśībhāvam ākhyāya prabhoḥ prabhāvam āha—taveti tribhiḥ | **vibhavo** mahimā | nanu brahmādayo **jagad-udayādi-**hetavo dṛśyante | tatrāha—viśveti | nanu brahma-rudrādi-bhaktāḥ sva-sva-sevyānām eva jagad-īśvaratvaṁ pratipādayanto mithaḥ spardhante ity ata āha—tatra mṛṣeti | **pṛthag-abhimatyā** vayaṁ hairaṇyagarbhāḥ śaivāḥ saurā ity-ādy-abhimānavantaḥ ||35||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.36 ||**

**paramāṇu-parama-mahatos**

**tvam ādy-antāntara-vartī traya-vidhuraḥ |**

**ādāv ante’pi ca sattvānāṁ**

**yad dhruvaṁ tad evāntarāle’pi ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tvam eva sṛṣṭy-ādi-kartety etad upapādayati—paramāṇuḥ sūkṣma-mūla-kāraṇam | parama-mahad antimaṁ kāryam | tayos tvam evādy-antāntara-vartī | ādāv ante cāntare madhye ca vartituṁ śīlaṁ yasya saḥ | ata eva traya-vidhura ādy-anta-madhya-śūnyo dhruvaḥ | te ca tvayā sṛjyante na tu dhruvāḥ | kuta ity ata āha—sattvānāṁ sattvena pratītānāṁ kāryāṇām ādāv ante’pi yad dhruvam anapāyy-antarāle’pi ca tad eva dhruvaṁ suvarṇādivat ||36||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tvam eva sṛṣṭy-ādi-kartā vāstava-vastu-rūpa ity upapādayati—paramāṇuḥ sūkṣmaṁ mūla-kāraṇam parama-mahad antimaṁ kāryam | tayos tvam evādy-antāntara-vartī | ādāv ante antare madhye ca vartituṁ śīlaṁ yasya saḥ | ata eva traya-vidhura ādy-anta-madhya-śūnyo nityaṁ, yataḥ sattvānāṁ kārya-vastūnām ādau ante ca yat dhruvaṁ kāraṇatvena sthiraṁ tad eva antarāle’pi suvarṇādivat | atas tvam eva sarva-kāraṇaṁ vāstavaṁ vastu anyat sarvaṁ kārya-jātam avāstavaṁ vastv ity arthaḥ ||36||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.37 ||**

**kṣity-ādibhir eṣa kilāvṛtaḥ**

**saptabhir daśa-guṇottarair aṇḍa-kośaḥ |**

**yatra pataty aṇu-kalpaḥ**

**sahāṇḍa-koṭi-koṭibhis tad anantaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **evaṁ dhruvatvena kālataḥ paricchedo nāstīty uktaṁ deśato’py aparicchedam āha—kṣity-ādibhir iti | pūrvasmāt pūrvasmād daśa-guṇam uttarottarair adhikair āvṛtaḥ | yatra tvayy aṇu-kalpo’ṇutulyaḥ patati paribhramati tat tasmād anantas tvam ||37||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **daśa-guṇā uttarottarā yeṣāṁ tairity arthaḥ ||37||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **evaṁ kālataḥ paricchedābhāvam uktvā deśato’py aparicchedam āha—kṣity-ādibhiḥ kṣiti-jala-teja-ākāśāhaṅkāra-mahat-tattva-prakṛtibhiḥ pūrvasmāt pūrvasmād daśa-guṇādhikair āvṛtaḥ | yatra tvayy aṇu-kalpaḥ patati paribhramati tat tasmād anantas tvam ||37||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.38 ||**

**viṣaya-tṛṣo nara-paśavo **

**ya upāsate vibhūtīr na paraṁ tvām |**

**teṣām āśiṣa īśa**

**tad anu vinaśyanti yathā rāja-kulam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yasmād evaṁ parameśvaras tvam evā’nye devās tava vibhūtayo’tas tvā vihāya viṣaya-kāmanayānyopāsakā ati-mandā ity-āha—viṣayeṣu tṛṭ tṛṣṇā yeṣāṁ te narākārāḥ paśavaḥ | kutaḥ, ye vibhūtīr indrādyā upāsate na tu paraṁ tvām | tataḥ kim ?tatrāha—teṣām iti | tad anu upāsya-nāśānantaram | yathā rāja-kulam anu rāja-kula-nāśān antaraṁ tat sevakānām āśiṣo naśyanti tadvat | ayaṁ ca paramo’vadhir madhye’pi naśyanty eva ||38||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **evaṁ prabhoḥ sarvotkarṣam ākhyāya bhaktasyāpi tam abhakta-nindayā prathamaṁ vyatirekeṇāha—viṣayeti | vibhūtīr indrādyāḥ, na tu tvām | upāsya-nāśānantaram | yathā rāja-kula-nāśānantaraṁ tat-sevakānām āśiṣo naśyanti ||38||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.39 ||**

**kāma-dhiyas tvayi racitā **

**na parama rohanti yathā karambha-bījāni |**

**jñānātmany aguṇamaye **

**guṇa-gaṇato’sya dvandva-jālāni ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **viṣaya-kāmenāpi kṛtā tvat sevā mokṣa-phalaivety āha—kāma-dhiyo viṣaya-kāmanā api he parama, tvayi racitāḥ kṛtāś cen na rohanti dehāntarotpattaye na bhavanti | karambha-bījāni bharjita-bījāni yathā | yato’sya jīvasya guṇa-gaṇād eva dvandva-samūhā bhavanti | ataḥ kāmenāpi nirguṇasya tava bhajanāc chanair nairguṇyaṁ bhavatīty arthaḥ ||39||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhaktasyotkarṣaṁ kaimutika-nyāyenānvayenāha—kāmā rājyādyās tad-artha-dhiyo matayas tvayi racitāḥ kṛtāś cet, na rohanti dehāntarotpattaye na bhavanti, yathā karambha-bījāni bhṛṣṭa-yava-bījāni, tathaiva | yadyapi kāma-dhiyo’nyatra rohantyo dṛṣṭāḥ bhṛṣṭa-bīja-tulyā na bhavanti, tad api viṣaya-sādguṇyād bhavantīty āha—jñānātmani cinmaye aguṇa-maye guṇa-mayāt padārthād bhinne | ato rasa-kūpa-patitaṁ vastu yathā rasa eva bhaved evaṁ tvayi praviṣṭāḥ kāma-dhiyo’pi cin-mayyo bhavatīti kathaṁ tāsāṁ saṁsāra-hetutvaṁ syād ity arthaḥ | yato guṇa-gaṇata eva dvandva-jālāni saṁsāra-kāraṇāni bhavanti ||39||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.40 ||**

**jitam ajita tadā bhavatā**

**yadāha bhāgavataṁ dharmam anavadyam |**

**niṣkiñcanā ye munaya**

**ātmārāmā yam upāsate’pavargāya ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **phala-kāmanayāpi tvad-ārādhanaṁ yadā mokṣa-hetus tadā kiṁ vaktavyaṁ bhagavad-dharma-māhātmyam ? iti vaktuṁ tat-saṁpradāya-pravartakatvena ca bhagavantaṁ stauti—jitam iti | **yadā bhavān bhāgavataṁ dharmam āha**, **tadā** he **bhagavan ! tvayā jitaṁ** sarvotkarṣeṇa sthitam | tatra hetuḥ—**ye niṣkiñcanāḥ** sanatkumārādayo **munayaḥ**, **te** yaṁ bhavantam **apavargāya **sevante tena bhavatā jitam | yaṁ dharmam iti vā ||40||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **jitam iti nijotkarṣa āviṣkṛtaḥ | bhagavann iti pāṭhaḥ svāmi-sammataḥ bhavateti tu prāyaḥ sarvatra ||40|| 

**bhakti-sandarbhaḥ** (120): aśeṣopadeṣṭur api tad-upadeśenaiva bhagavataḥ parama utkarṣa ucyate | yathā—jitam ajita iti | **jitam** ity atra **bhavatā** iti jñeyam | **āha** ity atra bhavān  iti ||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yady evaṁ sva-mahimnā sa-kāmāyā api bhakteḥ śraiṣṭhyaṁ, tadā kim uta niṣkāmāyāḥ ? kiṁ ca, bhakter niṣkāmatvaṁ ca tvat-pravartitam, ato niṣkāma-bhakter yat tava jayaḥ pūrva-pratipāditas tatrāpi parama-kṛpāluḥ sva-bhakta-vaśībhāvepsus tvam eva kāraṇam ity ato vastutas tavaiva viśeṣato jaya ity āha—jitam iti | 

he ajita ! **bhāgavataṁ dharmam anavadyaṁ** niṣkāmaṁ **yadaiva bhavān āha**, **tadaiva jitaṁ **bhavataiva bhaktā ṛṇīkṛtāḥ | yenaiva niṣkāma-bhakti-yogena bhaktair bhavān jīyate, tasya tvayaivoktatvāt tad-guṇaṁ, tvam eva sva-bhaktādhīnatvābhilāṣa-sādhakaṁ kṛpā-viśeṣam āsvādayantaḥ pratyuta eva bhaktāḥ svayam eva ṛṇībhūya sthitā bhavantīti bhāvaḥ | 

**ye niṣkiñcanāḥ** prathamata eva śuddhāḥ, tathā tat-saṅgatas tyakta-sva-niṣṭhā **munayas** tāpasā **ātmārāmā** jīvan-muktāś ca kecana **yam** eva dharmam **upāsate** | yad vā, niṣkiñcanā ity asyaiva viśeṣaṇa-dvayam | munayas tvan-manana-śīlā ātmārāmās tvayy eva ramamāṇā ity arthaḥ | 

**apavargāya** apakṛṣṭā vargāś catvāro’pi yatas tasmai premṇe apavargaś ca bhavati | yo’sāv [bhā.pu. 5.19.20] ity-ādi-pañcama-skandhīya-gadyokta-lakṣaṇāya bhakti-yogāyeti vā ||40||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.41 ||**

**viṣama-matir na yatra nṛṇāṁ**

**tvam aham iti mama taveti ca yad anyatra |**

**viṣama-dhiyā racito yaḥ**

**sa hy aviśuddhaḥ kṣayiṣṇur adharma-bahulaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **anavadyatām evāha—**viṣama-matir** **yatra** yasmin bhāgavate dharme **nāsti** | **yad anyatra** yathānyasmin kāmye dharme | nanu so’pi vedoktatvād anavadya eva ? tatrāha—**viṣama-dhiyā** śatru-maraṇādi-kāmanayā **racito **vihito yaḥ sa hy **aviśuddhaḥ,** rāga-dveṣādimattvāt, **kṣayiṣṇuś** ca naśvara-phalatvāt, **adharma-bahulaś** ca hiṁsādi-bāhulyāt | tad uktaṁ śabara-svāmibhiḥ—ubhayam iha codanāyāṁ lakṣyate’rtho’narthaś ca ity-ādi ||41||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yatra bhāgavate dharme tvam aham iti mama tava ity ahantāspada-mamatāspadayor **viṣama-matir** uttara-ślokārtha-dṛṣṭyā dveṣa-nibandhana-vaiṣamyavatī mama tava tvam ahaṁ śatrur iti matir **nāsti** yat, **yā anyatra** kāmya-dharme ity arthaḥ | kāmya-dharmam eva nindati—**viṣama-dhiyā** śatru-maraṇādi-kāmanayā **racito** **yaḥ** **sa hy aviśuddhaḥ** rāga-dveṣādi-mayatvāt, **kṣayiṣṇuś** ca naśvara-phalatvāt, **adharma-bahulaś** ca hiṁsādi-bāhulyāt | tad uktam śavara-svāminā—ubhayam iha codanāyāṁ lakṣyate’rtho’narthaś ca ity-ādi ||41||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.42 ||**

**kaḥ kṣemo nija-parayoḥ**

**kiyān vārthaḥ sva-para-druhādharmeṇa |**

**sva-drohāt tava kopaḥ**

**para-sampīḍayā ca tathādharmaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **etat prapañcayati—**kaḥ kṣemaḥ** kiṁ kuśalam ? na kiñcit | nija-parayoḥ **svasya parasya ca** sva-para-druhā, svasmai parasmai ca druhyatīti sva-para-dhruk, tena | yataḥ sva-drohād atyanta-kāya-kleśāt tava kopaḥ pīḍā sambhavati | tad uktaṁ gītāsu—


    karśayantaḥ śarīrasthaṁ bhūta-grāmam acetasaḥ |


    māṁ caivāntaḥ-śarīra-sthaṁ tān viddhy āsura-niścayān || [gītā 17.5] iti |

tathā **para-sampīḍayāadharmaḥ** | **ca**-śabdāt tava kopaś ca | atas tvayā rāgāndham api kathañcid veda-mārge pravartayituṁ kāmya-dharmo’bhihitona tattva-dṛṣṭyā ||42||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **nija-saṁsāra-hetutvāt sva-druhā pumān bhavābdhiṁ na taret, sa ātma-hetivatpaśv-ādy-upālambhāt para-druhāccetyarthaḥ | kopaḥ audāsya-mayaḥ krodhaḥ | **adharmo**’śuddho dharmaḥ ||42||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **uktam arthaṁ spaṣṭayati—**kaḥ kṣemaḥ** kiṁ kuśalam ? nija-parayor nijasyāhantāspadasyātmanaḥ parasya mamatāspadasya putra-kalatrāder na kiñcid ity arthaḥ |svasmai parasmai ca druhyatīti **sva-para-dhruk**, tena | yataḥ sva-drohāt para-hiṁsārthakātyanta-sva-kāya-kleśa-kara-tapo-vratādeḥ | **adharmaḥ** pāpaṁ tvat-kopaś ca ||42||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.43 ||**

**na vyabhicarati tavekṣā**

**yayā hy abhihito bhāgavato dharmaḥ |**

**sthira-cara-sattva-kadambeṣv**

**apṛthag-dhiyo yam upāsate tv āryāḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **bhāgavata-dharmeṇa tu na droha ity āha—neti | na vyabhicarati na paramārthaṁ jahāti | tava īkṣā dṛṣṭiḥ | avyabhicāre hetuḥ—sthireti | sthāvara-jaṅgama-prāni-samūheṣu sama-buddhayo bhāgavatā yaṁ dharmaṁ sevante ||43||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nanu kṣayiṣṇutvādi-doṣa-bāhulye’pi kāmya-dharme phala-darśanāt pravartate, nirdoṣe’pi niṣkāma-dharme phādarśanāt pravṛttausaṁśerate janās tatrāha—neti | tavekṣā mad-bhaktyā jīvaḥ kṛtārthībhavatīti parāmarśo na vyabhicaratīti kāmya-dharme kadācit phalasyāpi vyabhicāraḥ syān na tu tvadīyekṣāyāḥ | ata eva āryā ity anāryās tu saṁśeratāṁ nāmeti bhāvaḥ | apṛthag-dhiyaḥ svasya parasya ca sukha-duḥkheṣu pṛthag-buddhi-rahitā āryā iti āryākhyaṁ cchandaś cedam iti darśitam ||43||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.44 ||**

**na hi bhagavann aghaṭitam idaṁ**

**tvad-darśanān nṛṇām akhila-pāpa-kṣayaḥ |**

**yan-nāma sakṛc chravaṇāt**

**pukkaśo’pi vimucyate saṁsārāt**[^21]** ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **evam-bhūtasya bhāgavata-dharma-pravartakasya tava darśanāt sarva-pāpa-kṣayo bhavatīti kiṁ citram ity āha—nahīti ||44||

**sanātanaḥ **(ha.bha.vi. 11.486) : **sākṣāt**[^22] svayam eva vimukto bhavati, ity ananya-sādhanatoktā | yad vā, sākṣād iti vartamāna-tac-charīra evety arthaḥ | etac ca prārabdha-vināśitve pūrvaṁ likhitārtham eva ||44||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**bhakti-sandarbhaḥ (248)** : tādṛśasyāpi **sakṛc-chravaṇe’pi** mukti-phala-prāpteḥ, uttamasya tac-chravaṇe tu parama-bhaktir eva phalam ity abhipretam ||44|| 

**viśvanāthaḥ : **niṣkāma-dharmasya mayaiva sākṣāt phalaṁ labdham ity āha—na hīti | **nṛṇām** iti mamaiveti bhāvaḥ | pāpa-kṣayasya kā vārtā, mokṣo’pi bhavatīty āha—**yan-nāma** ekasyaiva, kim uta bahūnām ? **sakṛd** eva, kiṁ punar asakṛt ? **śravaṇād** eva, kim uta kīrtanādeḥ ? **pukkaśo’pi**, kim utānyaḥ ? **saṁsārād** eva, kim uta pāpād iti sādhanārambha eva phala-darśanam iti ||44||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.45 ||**

**atha bhagavan vayam adhunā**

**tvad-avaloka-parimṛṣṭāśaya-malāḥ |**

**sura-ṛṣiṇā yat kathitaṁ**

**tāvakena katham anyathā bhavati ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ato’haṁ kṛtārtho’smīty āha—atheti | atha ato hetoph tavāvalokanena parimṛṣṭā nirastā āśaye citte malā yeṣāṁ te | tvad-darśanaṁ ca mama nāradopadeśena jātam ity āha—sura-ṛṣiṇeti ||45||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ato’haṁ kṛtārtho’smīty āha—atheti ||45||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.46 ||**

**viditam ananta samastaṁ**

**tava jagad-ātmano janair ihācaritam |**

**vijñāpyaṁ parama-guroḥ**

**kiyad iva savitur iva khadyotaiḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yathā cāhaṁ pūrvam atimūḍha āsaṁ, yathā ca nāradenānugṛhīto’smi tat-sarvāntaryāminas tava mayā kiṁ prakāśanīyam ity āha—viditam iti | viśeṣeṇa jñāpyaṁ prakāśanīyaṁ kiyad iva na kim apīty arthaḥ | savitur yathā sva-dyotaiḥ prakāśanīyaṁ nāsti tadvat ||46||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **viṣayāndho’py ahaṁ sva-bhaktaṁ preṣya saṁsāra-kūpād uddhṛtya sva-caraṇāntikam ānīta ity-ādi kiṁ vijñāpayāmīty āha—viditam iti | savituḥ svatarīva tvayi khadyotair ivāsmābhiḥ kiṁ prakāśanīyam ||46||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.47 ||**

**namas tubhyaṁ bhagavate**

**sakala-jagat-sthiti-layodayeśāya |**

**duravasitātma-gataye**

**kuyogināṁ bhidā paramahaṁsāya ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ukta-lakṣaṇaṁ bhagavantaṁ praṇamati—nama iti dvābhyām | sakalasya jagataḥ sthity-ādīnām īśāya samarthāya | duravasitā’vijñātā ātma-gatir nija-tattvaṁ yasya tasmai | keṣām ? kuyoginām | kena ? bhidā bheda-dṛṣṭyā ||47||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **nama iti | bhidā nānopāsya-bheda-dṛṣṭyā kuyogināṁ duravasiteti | yad vā, bhidā bheda-mayyā bhaktyā | paramahaṁsāyeti pareṇānvayaḥ | tayā śuddha-rūpatvena hṛt-kamala-vihāriṇa ity arthaḥ ||47||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhidā bheda-dṛṣṭyā hetunā ye kuyoginas teṣāṁ paramahaṁsa-svarūpeṇoddhārakāyety arthaḥ ||47||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.48 ||**

**yaṁ vai śvasantam anu viśva-sṛjaḥ śvasanti**

**yaṁ cekitānam anu cittaya uccakanti |**

**bhū-maṇḍalaṁ sarṣapāyati yasya mūrdhni**

**tasmai namo bhagavate’stu sahasra-mūrdhne ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : śrīdharaḥ : **śvasanti ceṣṭante | cekitānaṁ paśyantam anu cittayo jñānendriyāṇi uccakanti svārūḍhaṁ paśyanti ||48||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **ucca-kanti svarūpaṁ paśyanti yasya eva jñāna-śakty-aṁśenaiva sva-sva-jñānaṁ labhanta ity arthaḥ | “kanīdipti-kānti-gatiṣu” ityasya yaṅ-lug-antasya rūpamidam ||48||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śvasantaṁ ceṣṭamānaṁ viśva-sṛjaḥ karmendriyāṇi śvasanti ceṣṭante, yaṁ cekitānaṁ paśyantaṁ cittayaḥ jñānendriyāṇi uccakanti sva-sva-viṣayaṁ paśyanti ||48||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.49 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**saṁstuto bhagavān evam anantas tam abhāṣata |**

**vidyādhara-patiṁ prītaś citraketuṁ kurūdvaha ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.50 ||**

**śrī-bhagavān uvāca—**

**yan nāradāṅgirobhyāṁ te vyāhṛtaṁ me’nuśāsanam |**

**saṁsiddho’si tayā rājan vidyayā darśanāc ca me ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **me’nuśāsanaṁ mad-viṣaya upadeśaḥ | tena tayā ca vidyayā’smāc ca darśanāt saṁsiddho’si ||50||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **me’nuśāsanaṁ śravaṇa-kīrtanādi-bhajanaṁ tena tayā, vidyayā nāradopadiṣṭa-mahā-mantreṇa ca tat-sādhyān mama darśanāc ca ||50||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.51 ||**

**ahaṁ vai sarva-bhūtāni bhūtātmā bhūta-bhāvanaḥ |**

**śabda-brahma paraṁ brahma mamobhe śāśvatī tanū ||**

**madhvaḥ : **haris tu sarva-bhūtāni tad-antaryāmy-apekṣayā |


    tiṅ-padāny api sarvāṇi sup-padāni tathaiva ca |


    tasminn eva pravarteta mukhyā vṛttyā viśeṣataḥ || iti ca ||51||

**śrīdharaḥ : **tad bodha-dārḍhyāya svayam apy upadiśati, aham ity-ādinā | sarva-bhūtāny aham eva bhūtānām ātmā bhoktāpy aham eva | bhoktṛ-bhogyātmakaṁ viśvaṁ mad-vyatiriktaṁ nāstīty arthaḥ | yato’haṁ bhūta-bhāvanaḥ bhūtānāṁ prakāśakaḥ kāraṇaṁ ca | 

nanu śabda-brahma prakāśakaṁ, paraṁ brahma kāraṇaṁ ca prakāśakaṁ ca ? satyam, te ubhe mamaiva rūpe ity āha—śabda-brahmeti | śāśvatī śāśvatyau ||51||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **aham iti | atra śabda-brahmaṇaḥ sāhacaryāt para-brahmaṇo’pyaṁśatvam āyāti||51||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kiṁ ca, bhakti-tattvaṁ tvayā jñātam eva, tatra ajita jitaḥ [bhā.pu. 6.16.35] ity-ādi-stutir eva pramāṇam | jijñāsā-nairapekṣyārthaṁ jñāna-tattvam aham evopadiśāmi, śṛṇv ity āha—ahaṁ vai iti | atredaṁ vivecanīyam | vastu tāvat dvividhaṁ—vāstavam avāstavaṁ ca | brahma paramātmā bhagavān sa-parikara ity etat tritayam eva vāstavaṁ vastu, māyika-prapañca-jātam idam avāstavaṁ vastu | avastu ca dvividhaṁ—kāryam akāryaṁ ca | kāryaṁ svapnendra-jālādi-gatam | akāryaṁ khapuṣpa-śaśaśṛṅgādi | eṣāṁ madhye, vedyaṁ vāstavam atra vastu [bhā.pu. 1.1.2] iti prathamokter vāstava-vastuna evopādeyatvaṁ vaktuṁ, prathamam avāstavaṁ vastv āha—**sarva-bhūtāni** bhoktṛ-bhogyātmakāni jaganti aham eva, madīya-jīva-śakti-māyā-śakti-mayatvād iti bhāvaḥ | atra jīvānām avāstava-vastutvam avidyāvṛtatvād evoktam | 

vāstavaṁ vastv āha—**bhūtānāṁ** samaṣṭi-vyaṣṭīnām **ātmā** antaryāmīti dvitīyaḥ | tṛtīyaś ca puruṣo’ham | tathā **bhūtāni** tāni bhāvayatīty utpādayatīti prathamaḥ puruṣaś cāham | tathā bhūtāni dāsya-sakhyādi-bhāvavanti karotīti **bhūta-bhāvanaḥ,** kṛṣṇo rāmaś ca samprati tvayā dṛśyaś cāham | 

kiṁ ca, niśvāsa-rūpaṁ yat **śabda-brahma** vedaḥ, tathā man-nirviśeṣākāratvena jñāniṣu pratipadyamānaṁ yat **paraṁ brahma**, **te ubhe** mamaiva **tanu**-rūpe | vedasya śabda-rūpatvād ākāśa-guṇatvenānitya-śaṅkāyās tathā para-brahmaṇaś cānirdeśyatvenāvastutva-śaṅkāyā vāraṇāyāha—**śāśvatī** śāśvatyau nitya-satye eva ||51||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.52 ||**

**loke vitatam ātmānaṁ lokaṁ cātmani santatam |**

**ubhayaṁ ca mayā vyāptaṁ mayi caivobhayaṁ kṛtam ||**

**madhvaḥ : **lokaṁ cātmani santataṁ vāsanā-rūpeṇa ||52||

**śrīdharaḥ : **atas tam evaṁ paśyety āha—loke bhogya-prapañce bhoktṛtvena vitatam anugatam ātmānaṁ, lokaṁ cātmani bhogyatvena santataṁ vyāptam | tad ubhayaṁ ca mayā kāraṇātmanā vyāptam | mayi caivobhayaṁ kṛtaṁ prakalpitaṁ smared iti tṛtīyenānvayaḥ | paśyed ity adhyāhāro vā ||52||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **tathaivānubhāvayati—loka iti | ātmānaṁ paraṁ brahma svarūpaṁvitatam āśrayatvena vartamānam, ātmani tasmin santatam āśritaṁ paśya mayā bhagavad-rūpeṇa para-brahmaṇo’pi madīya-nirviśeṣāvirbhāva-rūpatvāt | ata evobhayaṁ ca mayi kṛtaṁ maj-jñāna-nimittam eva nirūpitam ity arthaḥ ||52||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nanu tvam eva cet sarvaṁ bhavasi, tarhi kiṁ sarva-bhūtāny evopāsyatvena dhyeyāni bhaktānām utāntaryāmy-ādi-rūpāṇi ? iti tatrāha—loke bhogya-prapañce bhoktṛtvena vitatam anugatam ātmānaṁ,jīvaṁ tathā lokaṁ cātmani bhogyatvena santataṁ sa-vistāram upasthitam | tad ubhayaṁ mayā kāraṇātmanā vyāptam | mayi cādhiṣṭhāna-kāraṇe ubhayaṁ kṛtaṁ kārya-rūpaṁ smared iti tṛtīyenānvayaḥ | tena sarva-bhūtāni mac-chakti-kāryāṇy anityāny asvarūpa-bhūtāni nopāsyatvena dhyeyānīti bhāvaḥ ||52||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.53-54 ||**

**yathā suṣuptaḥ puruṣo viśvaṁ paśyati cātmani |**

**ātmānam eka-deśa-sthaṁ manyate svapna utthitaḥ ||**

**evaṁ jāgaraṇādīni jīva-sthānāni cātmanaḥ |**

**māyā-mātrāṇi vijñāya tad-draṣṭāraṁ paraṁ smaret ||**

**madhvaḥ : **māyā-mātrāṇi prakṛti-nirmitāni ||54||

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu jāgrad-ādy-avasthā-bhedena bhoktṛ-bhogyātmakaṁ viśvaṁ sphuṭaṁ pratīyamānaṁ kathaṁ kalpitaṁ syāt ? ity āśaṅkya svapna-gata-jāgrad-ādi-dṛṣṭāntena saṁbhāvayann āha—yatheti dvābhyām | yathā svapne supto viśvaṁ giri-vanādi-rūpaṁ deśāntara-stham ātmany eva paśyati | svapna-madhye suṣuptiṁ svapnaṁ ca paśyatīty arthaḥ | tathā svapna evotthitaḥ sannātmaṇam eka-deśa-sthaṁ śayana-deśe sthitaṁ manyate, jāgrad-avasthām anubhavati ||53|| evaṁ prasiddhāny api jāgarādīni jīva-sthānāni jīvopādher buddher avasthā-bhūtāny ātmano māyā-mātrāṇīty evaṁ vijñāya, teṣāṁ draṣṭāram ata eva paraṁ tad-avasthā-rahitam ātmānaṁ smaret ||54||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **nanu, yāvadviśvasmādanāsakto na syāt, tāvat kathaṁ syāt ? ityevam āśaṅkya śuddha-jīvasya svarūpa-jñāna-pūrvakaṁ taj-jñānam upadiśati—yatheti yugmakena | ayam arthaḥ—yathā svapna-madhya eva suṣuptaḥ kaścit puruṣaḥ punaḥ svapnaṁ paśyan bhrama-viśeṣeṇa viśvaṁ giri-vanādikam ātmani paśyati, svasminnevāropayati, punastasminneva svapne utthito labdha-jāgara iva san ātmānam eka-deśa-sthaṁ tatra śayanaika-deśaṁ paśyan tad-giri-vanādikaṁ bhinnam eva paśyati, tāni jāgarādīni yathā ātmanaḥ paramātmano mama māyā-mātrāṇi santi, jīva-sthānāni vijñāya vijñātasya puruṣasya śuddha-jīvasyāpi draṣṭāraṁ mām eva paraṁ smarediti ||53||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **pratyuta tāny avāstava-vastūni khalv avastūnīva tyaktvā mamāntaryāmy-ādi-rūpam evopāsītety āha—yatheti dvābhyām | svapne svapna-madhye eva suṣuptaḥ suṣṭhu suptaḥ puruṣaḥ svapnaṁ paśyan bhrama-viśeṣeṇa viśvaṁ giri-vanādikam ātmani paśyati svasmin evāropayati | punas tasminn eva svapne utthito labdha-jāgaraḥ sann ātmānam eka-deśa-sthaṁ tatra śayanaika-pradeśa-sthaṁ manyate, jāgrad-avasthām anubhavan, tad-giri-vanādikaṁ bhinnam eva manyate ity arthaḥ | 

tad evam avastu-bhūtaḥ svāpniko jāgaro yathā tathaiva prasiddho vastu-bhūto’pi jāgaro jñeyo naśvaratvād ity āha—evam iti | jīva-sthānāni jīvopādher buddher evāvasthāś ca ātma5 parameśvarasya māyā-śakti-kāryatvān māyā-mātrāṇi jñātvā teṣāṁ draṣṭāraṁ paraṁ śreṣṭham antaryāmiṇam iti jīvātmā vyāvṛttaḥ | 

atra svāpnikye jāgara-svapna-suṣupty-avasthā avidyayā jīvena sṛjyatvād avidyā-mātryo hy avastu-bhūtā evaṁ prasiddhā jāgarādy-avasthās tu māyā-śaktyā bhagavatā sṛṣṭā māyā-mātryaḥ khalv avastu-bhūtā eva, tathāpi svāpnikaṁ giri-vana-sarpa-vyāghra-hasty-aśvādikas tv avidyayā jīvena sṛjyam avastv eveti vivecanīyam ||53||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.55 ||**

**yena prasuptaḥ puruṣaḥ svāpaṁ vedātmanas tadā |**

**sukhaṁ ca nirguṇaṁ brahma tam ātmānam avehi mām ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu teṣāṁ draṣṭāram iti katham ucyate, svāpe dṛśyābhāvena draṣṭṛtvābhāvāt tatrāha—yeneti | prasuptaḥ puruṣo jīvo yena rūpeṇa tadā svāpa-kāle ātmanaḥ svāpaṁ nirguṇam atīndriyaṁ sukhaṁ ca veda tam ātmānaṁ brahma mām avehi | tadā svāpa-sukhayor asaṁvedane “sukham aham asvāpsam” iti smṛter asaṁbhavāt ||55||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **tam eva spaṣṭayati—yeneti | māyikāhaṅkārālaye jīvādi-gata-mahā-cic-chakty-aṁśena tattva-viśeṣeṇa hetunā svāpaḥ tatra nirguṇa-sukhaṁ ca veda, tadbrahmāvehi | ātmānaṁ paramātmānaṁ māṁ bhagavad-rūpaṁ cāvehi | vadanti tattattva-vida [bhā.pu. 1.2.11] ityādeḥ ||55||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nanu taṁ draṣṭāram antaryāmiṇaṁ katham ahaṁ jānāmi ? ity ata āha—yeneti | prasuptaḥ puruṣo jīvo yadā svāpaṁ veda, tad eva suṣuptāv ātma5 svasya nirguṇaṁ nirviśeṣaṁ sukhaṁ ca yenaiva hetunā veda, tam ātmānam antaryāmiṇam avehi | yatraiva guṇair dṛḍha-baddham āvṛta-jñānānandam api jīvaṁ kṛpayā suṣuptau nityam eva guṇān pravilāpya nirguṇaṁ tadīyaṁ sukhaṁ tam anubhāvayati | sa evāntaryāmī spaṣṭam evāvagamyatāṁ, na hi taṁ vinā hy asvatantro jīvaḥ svayam eva sva-bandhanaṁ vimocya svīya-sukhaṁ draṣṭuṁ śaknuyād iti bhāvaḥ | tam antaryāmiṇam eva nirviśeṣatvena pratītaṁ brahma avehi | brahmaiva sa-viśeṣaṁ māṁ bhagavantam avehi | eka evāhaṁ brahma paramātma bhagavān iti tri-rūpo bhavāmi, na tu mat-svarūpasya dvitvaṁ tritvaṁ vā | yad uktaṁ devaiḥ—svarūpa-dvayābhāvāt [bhā.pu. 6.9.36] iti ||55||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.56 ||**

**ubhayaṁ smarataḥ puṁsaḥ prasvāpa-pratibodhayoḥ |**

**anveti vyatiricyeta taj jñānaṁ brahma tat param ||**

**madhvaḥ : **pratibodheneti svayam api pratibuddhaḥ suptāv asvapan vyatiricyeta ||56||

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu svāpa-sākṣiṇā dṛṣṭaṁ kathaṁ jāgrad-avasthaḥ smaret ? na hy anyena dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati tatrāha—ubhayaṁ prasvāpaṁ pratibodhaṁ ca smarato’nusandadhataḥ | tayoḥ prasvāpa-pratibodhayoḥ prakāśakatvena yad anveti tābhyāṁ vyatiricyeta ca | ekaikāpāye’py anapāyāt | taj jñānaṁ paraṁ brahma tad eva, na tu bhinnam ity arthaḥ | ato bālye dṛṣṭasya yauvane smṛtivadavasthāntaratve’pi svāpānandayoḥ smaraṇaṁ ghaṭata iti bhāvaḥ | tad evaṁ-bhūtaṁ brahmātmānam avehīty anuṣaṅgaḥ ||56||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **ataeva jīva-jñānasyāpi brahmaṇi tātparyam ity āha—ubhayam iti | taj-jñānaṁ śuddha-jīva-svarūpaṁ tacca brahmaṇi tat-param iti ||56||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nanu svāpa-sākṣiṇā dṛṣṭaṁ jāgrad-avasthaḥ kathaṁ “sukham aham asvāpsam iti smaret ? na hy anyena dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati | tatrāha—ubhayaṁ prasvāpaṁ pratibodhaṁ ca smarato’nusandadhataḥ puṁsas tayoḥ prasvāpa-pratibodhayoḥ yad anveti, tābhyāṁ vyatiricyeta, ekaikāpāye’py anapāyāt | taj jñānaṁ jīva ity arthaḥ | ato bālye dṛṣṭasya yauvane smṛtivadavasthāntaratve’pi svāpānandayoḥ smaraṇaṁ ghaṭata iti bhāvaḥ | tat paraṁ tato jīvāt paraṁ brahma, na tu sa eva brahmety arthaḥ | jīvasya taṭastha-śaktitvena tad-rūpatve’pi tasya svarūpa-śaktitvābhāvāt | ato bhinnam eva brahmety arthaḥ ||56||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.57 ||**

**yad etad vismṛtaṁ puṁso mad-bhāvaṁ bhinnam ātmanaḥ |**

**tataḥ saṁsāra etasya dehād deho mṛter mṛtiḥ ||**

**madhvaḥ : **sarva-bhinnaṁ paramātmānaṁ vismaran saṁsared iha |


    abhinnaṁ saṁsmaran yāti tamo nāsty atra saṁśayaḥ || iti ca ||57||

**śrīdharaḥ : **vipakṣe doṣam āha—yad yadi etan mad-bhāvaṁ mat-svarūpaṁ brahma vismṛtaṁ tad ātmanaḥ sakāśād bhinnaṁ bhavati | tata etasya puṁsaḥ saṁsāro bhavati | saṁsāra-svarūpam āha—dehād deho janmānantaraṁ punar janma mṛter anantaraṁ mṛtiś ceti ||57||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **tad-ajñāne doṣamāha—yadyasmādbrahma vismṛtam | anādy-ajñānenānusaṁhitam | tatastasmādeva etasya jīvasya saṁsāraḥ taccābhiprāya-viśeṣeṇa jīvādbhinnatvena svasmādbhinnatvena darśayati—ātmanobhinnaṁ, mama bhāvaḥ sattā yatra taditi bhayaṁ dvitīyābhiniveśataḥ syāt [bhā.pu. 11.2.37] ity-āderyuktam eva tadajñāne saṁsāra iti ||57||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ato brahma-jīvayoḥ svarūpaikya-bhāvanam evāparādho’nartha-hetur ity āha—yad etad iti | ātmano jīvāt sakāśāt mad-bhāvaṁ mat-svarūpaṁ bhinnam eva klībatvam ārṣam | yad yadi vismṛtaṁ syād abhinnam eva syāt, tato hetor etasyābhinna-darśinaḥ puṁsaḥ saṁsāraḥ syāt | saṁsāram evāha—dehād iti | ata eva tattvam asīty ādau jīvasya tadīya-taṭastha-śaktitvena tādrūpyād eva sūrya-tat-kiraṇayor ivaikyaṁ bhāvanīyam iti bhāvaḥ | tad evam avāstava-vastuno viśvasya tac-chakti-kāryatvenābhinnatvāt tādrūpyam | tādrūpyeti tātsvarūpyābhāvād bhinnam eva naśvaratva-prayojakam | śuddha-jīvasya tv anaśvaratvād vāstava-vastv-antaḥ-pātitve’pi taṭastha-śaktitvāt tādrūpyam eva, na tu tātsvarūpyaṁ, brahma-paramātma-bhagavatāṁ tu vāstava-vastutvaṁ svarūpaikyādy aikyaṁ ca | bhagavan-nitya-preyasī-pārṣada-dhāmnāṁ cic-chakti-vilāsatvāt | keṣāñcin nitya-siddhatvād api vāstava-vastutvaṁ tātsvarūpyaṁ ca | keṣāñcin nitya-mukta-bhaktatvena, keṣāñcil labdha-bhakti-kaivalyatvena siddhānāṁ dāsyādi-vāsanāvatāṁ jīvānāṁ tu nitya-dāsādi-gaṇāntaḥ-pātitvābhāvena svarūpa-śaktyānāviṣṭatvād eva tātsvarūpyam | labdha-bhakti-prādhānyena siddhānāṁ jīvānāṁ śāstra-bhaktatvāt dāsādi-gaṇāntaḥ-pātitvābhāvena svarūpa-śaktyānāviṣṭatvāt tādrūpyaṁ vāstava-vastutvaṁ ceti bhagavato’neka-śaktimatvenādvaitaṁ phalitam iti prasaṅgāt vaiṣṇava-siddhānto darśitaḥ ||57||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.58 ||**

**labdhveha mānuṣīṁ yoniṁ jñāna-vijñāna-sambhavām |**

**ātmānaṁ yo na buddhyeta na kvacit kṣemam āpnuyāt ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yony-antare’pi bhogādi-saṁpādanaṁ śakyaṁ jñānārthaṁ tv atraiva yatitavyam ity āha—labdhveti | jñānaṁ śāstroktam, vijñānam aparokṣam, tayoḥ saṁbhavo yasyāṁ tām ||58||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ukta-lakṣaṇa-jñānārtham avaśyam eva yatitavyam ity āha—labdhveti | jñānaṁ śāstrotthaṁ, vijñānam aparokṣaṁ, tayoḥ sambhavo yasyāṁ tām, ātmānaṁ jīvaṁ parameśvaraṁ ca ||58||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.59 ||**

**smṛtvehāyāṁ parikleśaṁ tataḥ phala-viparyayam |**

**abhayaṁ cāpy anīhāyāṁ saṅkalpād viramet kaviḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **vairāgyārtham āha—īhāyāṁ pravṛtti-mārge | tata īhātaḥ | anīhāyāṁ nivṛtti-mārge tv abhayaṁ mokṣo bhavatīti ca smṛtvā phala-saṅkalpād viramet | pāṭhāntare nobhayaṁ parikleśaḥ phala-viparyayaś ca nāstīty evaṁ smṛtvā ||59||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **etaj jñānecchur jñāta-dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa-karma-phalakaḥ karma-niṣṭhāṁ tyajed ity āha—īhāyāṁ sakāmatve tata īhātaḥ | anīhāyāṁ niṣkāmatve abhayaṁ sarvata eva bhayābhāvaḥ | nobhayam iti pāṭhe kleśa-viparyayau na syātām iti smṛtaḥ ||59||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.60 ||**

**sukhāya duḥkha-mokṣāya kurvāte dampatī kriyāḥ |**

**tato’nivṛttir aprāptir duḥkhasya ca sukhasya ca ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : **etad vivṛṇoti—sukhāyeti tribhiḥ | duḥkhasyānivṛttiḥ sukhasyāprāptiḥ ||60||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.61 ||**

**evaṁ viparyayaṁ buddhvā nṛṇāṁ vijñābhimāninām |**

**ātmanaś ca gatiṁ sūkṣmāṁ sthāna-traya-vilakṣaṇām ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **vijñā udyame-pravīṇā vayam ity abhimānavatām | sthāna-traya-vilakṣaṇāṁ turīyāṁ buddhvā ||61||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **pūrvānurūpam evopasaṁharati—evam iti yūgmakena | ātmārāmāś ca munayaḥ [bhā.pu. 1.7.10] ity-ādeḥ ||61||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sthāna-traya-vilakṣaṇāṁ turīyām ||61||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.62 ||**

**dṛṣṭa-śrutābhir mātrābhir nirmuktaḥ svena tejasā |**

**jñāna-vijñāna-santṛpto mad-bhaktaḥ puruṣo bhavet ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : dṛṣṭa-śrutābhir mātrābhir** aihikāmuṣmikair viṣayaiḥ | **svena tejasā** viveka-balena ||62||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : mātrābhir** viṣayaiḥ | **sva-tejasā** svīya-sādhana-prabhāveṇa ||62||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.63 ||**

**etāvān eva manujair yoga-naipuṇya-buddhibhiḥ |**

**svārthaḥ sarvātmanā jñeyo yat parātmaika-darśanam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **na cātaḥ paraḥ puruṣārtho’stīty āha—etāvān iti | **yoge naipuṇyaṁ** yasyāṁ sā **buddhir** yeṣām | **parasyātmana ekaṁ darśanam** iti **yad etāvān eva** ||63||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **tad eva praśaṁsati—etāvān iti | **paramātmano** bhagavata **evaikaṁ** kevalaṁ **darśanam** anubhava iti yat ||63|| [prīti-sandarbhaḥ, 2]

**viśvanāthaḥ : parasya** śreṣṭhasya **ātmanaḥ** paramātmana **eva ekaṁ darśanaṁ**, na tu viṣayasya ||63||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.64 ||**

**tvam etac chraddhayā rājann apramatto vaco mama |**

**jñāna-vijñāna-sampanno dhārayann āśu sidhyasi ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **saṁsiddho ’sīti | yat pūrvam uktam adhunā ca siddhyasīti tad dvayam api vartamāna-sāmīpyenaiva jñeyaṁ | tatrāpy apramattaḥ san mama vaco dhārayann iti bhāvi-vighno hetur apy uddiṣṭaḥ ||64||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.16.65 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**āśvāsya bhagavān itthaṁ citraketuṁ jagad-guruḥ |**

**paśyatas tasya viśvātmā tataś cāntardadhe hariḥ ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ṣaṣṭhasya ṣoḍaśo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

—o)0(o—

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ ṣaṣṭha-skandhe

citraketūpākhyāne

ṣoḍaśo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 6.16 ||

(6.17)


### atha saptadaśo’dhyāyaḥ


## citraketūpākhyāne

**|| 6.17.1 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**yataś cāntarhito’nantas tasyai kṛtvā diśe namaḥ |**

**vidyādharaś citraketuś cacāra gagane caraḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **

tataḥ saptadaśe’moghamahārdhi prāpya khe caran |

vihasya giriśaṁ śāpād umāyā vṛtratāṁ gataḥ ||

yato yasyām | tasyai diśe namaḥ namanaṁ kṛtvā ||1||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **

citraketuḥ saptadaśe vidyādhara-patir bhavan |

vihasya śaṅkaraṁ devyāḥ śāpato vṛtratām agāt ||

yato yasyām diśi ||1||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.2 ||**

**sa lakṣaṁ varṣa-lakṣāṇām avyāhata-balendriyaḥ |**

**stūyamāno mahā-yogī munibhiḥ siddha-cāraṇaiḥ ||**

**kulācalendra-droṇīṣu nānā-saṅkalpa-siddhiṣu |**

**reme vidyādhara-strībhir gāpayan harim īśvaram ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : sa** citraketur **vidyādhara-strībhir hariṁ gāpayan rema** iti dvayor anvayaḥ | **avyāhataṁ balamindriya**-pāṭavaṁ ca yasya ||2|| **nānā**-vidhāḥ **saṅkalpenaivasiddhayo** yāsu tāsu ||3||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **sa lakṣam iti yugmakam |_|_2||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nānā-saṅkalpa-siddhiṣv api saṅkalpān vihāya hariṁ gāpayann eva reme harer guṇa-caraṇāravinda-kīrtanayor eva rato’bhūd ity arthaḥ ||2-3||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.4 ||**

**ekadā sa vimānena viṣṇu-dattena bhāsvatā |**

**giriśaṁ dadṛśe gacchan parītaṁ siddha-cāraṇaiḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **

akasmād adbhutaiśvarya-garvāt prācīna-karmataḥ |

āsurīṁ yonim āpanno bhavān īśāpataḥ sa tu ||

tad āha—ekadety-ādinā ||4||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **tatrāpi prācīna-mahad-aparādhāntarasya duṣphalatvam āha—ekadeti ||4||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **

bhaktiṁ bhūtiṁ harir dattvā sva-vicchedānubhūtaye |

devyāḥ śāpena vṛtratvaṁ nītvā taṁ svāntike’nayat ||

asvīkṛtāṁ sva-dehārdhīkṛtām ||4||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.5 ||**

**āliṅgyāṅkīkṛtāṁ devīṁ bāhunā muni-saṁsadi |**

**uvāca devyāḥ śṛṇvantyā jahāsoccais tad-antike ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **aṅkī-kṛtām utsaṅgenaikī-kṛtya devīṁ bāhunāliṅgya sthitam | uvāca jahāsa ca | tasyāntike sthitaḥ san ||5||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.6 ||**

**citraketur uvāca—**

**eṣa loka-guruḥ sākṣād dharmaṁ vaktā śarīriṇām |**

**āste mukhyaḥ sabhāyāṁ vai mithunī-bhūya bhāryayā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **dharmaṁ vaktā vadati | śarīriṇāṁ madhye mukhyaś ca bhāryayā mithunībhūya cāste ||6||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.7 ||**

**jaṭā-dharas tīvra-tapā brahmavādi-sabhā-patiḥ |**

**aṅkīkṛtya striyaṁ cāste gata-hrīḥ prākṛto yathā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **prākṛto yatheti, na tu prākṛtaḥ sākṣād īśvaratvād iti dakṣavan nāyaṁ śiva-nindako’parādhī jñeya iti bhāvaḥ ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.8 ||**

**prāyaśaḥ prākṛtāś cāpi striyaṁ rahasi bibhrati |**

**ayaṁ mahā-vrata-dharo bibharti sadasi striyam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mahā-vrata-dharo naiṣṭhika-brahmacārī yogīndraḥ priyaṁ bibhartīty acintyam aiśvaryam iti bhāvaḥ ||8||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.9 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**bhagavān api tac chrutvā prahasyāgādha-dhīr nṛpa |**

**tūṣṇīṁ babhūva sadasi sabhyāś ca tad-anuvratāḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **agādhā gambhīrā dhīr yasya saḥ ||9||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **agādhe anavagāha-mahimni bhagavati dhīr buddhir yasya saḥ | ataḥ śarīrādāvanāveśāt tūṣṇīṁ babhūveti | tad-anuvratā iti | atas tad-abhiprāyānusāreṇaiva te ca tad-anugāś ca tuṣṇīṁbabhūvur ity arthaḥ ||9||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **prahasyeti | mām api sad-ācāre sthāpayitum icchatīti bhāvaḥ | sahasaiva citraketor abhiprāya-jñānād agādhā sarvair duṣpraveśā dhīr yasya saḥ | citraketor abhiprāyaś cāyam—ayaṁ khalv īśvara eva nāsya durācāratve’pi kṣatiḥ | yaḥ khalv anabhijñaḥimaṁ nindiṣyati tasyāparādhāt sarva-nāśo bhaviṣyati, yathā dakṣasyety ata imam adyārabhyāpi yadi sadācāre sthāpayitum ahaṁ śaknuyām, tadā lokānāṁ bhadraṁ syāt | tathā viṣṇuḥ parameśvaro bhadra eva sucaritatvāt | rudras tv abhadro durācāratvād ity apratiṣṭhāpyasya na bhaved iti | tad asmai hitaiṣiṇe kaṭhora-bhāṣiṇe’pi hari-bhaktāya nāhaṁ kupyāmīti bhagavataḥ śambhor abhiprāyānusāriṇaḥ sabhyāś ca tūṣṇīṁ babhūvur eva na tu cukrudhuḥ | śrī-śiva-nindanasya tad-abhipretatve te sabhyā sadya eva karṇau pidhāya tato nirayāsyann iti jñeyam | yad uktaṁ—bhagavan-nindanaṁ śrutvā tat-parasya janasya vā ity-ādi ||9||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.10 ||**

**ity atad-vīrya-viduṣi bruvāṇe bahv-aśobhanam |**

**ruṣāha devī dhṛṣṭāya nirjitātmābhimānine ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **na tasya vīryaṁ prabhāvaṁ vidvān atad-vīrya-vidvāṁs tasmin | nirjitātmābhimānine jitendriyo’ham ity abhimānavate iti ruṣā krodhenāha ||10||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **devī tu na kṣantuṁ śaktavatīty āha—ity atad-vīryeti | vīrya-mātraṁ tādṛśa-laukika-cāritryāc cāditaṁ yan mahā-bhāgavatatvaṁ tad apy aviduṣīty arthaḥ | tathaivoktaṁ—agādha-dhīḥ iti ||10||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **na tasya vīryaṁ prabhāvaṁ vettīti tasmin na hi svatantra īśvaraḥ kasyacid api śikṣayākim api karotīti bhāvaḥ | aśobhanaṁ bruvāṇe iti jagadīśvare nīti śikṣaṇānaucityāt dhṛṣṭāya niḥśaṅka-bhāṣitvād atipragalbhāya niḥśeṣeṇa jito mayā prema-vaśīkṛtaḥ ātmā paramātmā saṅkarṣaṇo’pīty abhimānavate | ruṣeti tu mahādeva-sabhyayor abhiprāyasyājñānād eva ruḍ iyam iti na vyākhyeyā | kintu bahu-bruvāṇa iti hitam apy etad asmad anupāditsitam ayaṁ naika-dvān vārān nāpi tri-caturān, kintu bahūn eva vārān brūte iti krodhe kāraṇaṁ jñeyam ||10||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.11 ||**

**śrī-pārvaty uvāca—**

**ayaṁ kim adhunā loke śāstā daṇḍa-dharaḥ prabhuḥ |**

**asmad-vidhānāṁ duṣṭānāṁ nirlajjānāṁ ca viprakṛt ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **viruddhaṁ prakarṣeṇa karotīti viprakṛt ||11||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **viśeṣeṇa prakarṣaṁ karotīti viprakṛt śāsanena hitakṛd ity arthaḥ ||11||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.12 ||**

**na veda dharmaṁ kila padmayonir**

**na brahma-putrā bhṛgu-nāradādyāḥ |**

**na vai kumāraḥ kapilo manuś ca**

**ye no niṣedhanty ati-vartinaṁ haram ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ati-vartinaṁ śāstram atikramya vartana-śīlam | ye no niṣedhanti na nivārayanti ||12||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.13 ||**

**eṣām anudhyeya-padābja-yugmaṁ**

**jagad-guruṁ maṅgala-maṅgalaṁ svayam |**

**yaḥ kṣatra-bandhuḥ paribhūya sūrīn**

**praśāsti dhṛṣṭas tad ayaṁ hi daṇḍyaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **eṣāṁ brahmādīnām anudhyeyaṁ padābja-yugmaṁ yasya tam | maṅgala-maṅgalaṁ parama-dharma-mūrtim | sūrīn paribhūyājñān kṛtvā jagad-guruṁ yaḥ praśāsti | tat tasmāt ||13||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **eṣāmityasya ṭīkāyām avajñāṁ kṛtveti pāṭhe teṣām iti śeṣaḥ | ajñān kṛtveti ajñān matvetyarthaḥ |_|_13||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **paribhūya muhur api kaṭhoroktyā tiraskṛtya sūrīn etat sabhāsado’py anabhijñān jñātvā paribhūya jagad-guruṁ praśāsti ||13||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.14 ||**

**nāyam arhati vaikuṇṭha- pāda-mūlopasarpaṇam |**

**sambhāvita-matiḥ stabdhaḥ sādhubhiḥ paryupāsitam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu hari-bhakto’yaṁ daṇḍārha iti cet tatrāha—nāyaṁ sādhubhiḥ parisevitaṁ vaikuṇṭhasya pāda-mūlopasarpaṇam arhati | yataḥ saṁbhāvitā aham adhika iti kṛtā matir yena | ata eva stabdho’namraḥ ||14||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sambhāvitā ahaṁ mahā-bhakta ity abhimānavatī matir yasya saḥ ||14||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.15 ||**

**ataḥ pāpīyasīṁ yonim āsurīṁ yāhi durmate |**

**yatheha bhūyo mahatāṁ na kartā putra kilbiṣam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tad evaṁ svayaṁ daṇḍyatvaṁ niścitya taṁ prāha—ata iti | he **putra** ! **yathā bhūyo mahatāṁ kilbiṣam** aparādhaṁ **na kartā** na kariṣyasi, tathā **yāhi** ity arthaḥ ||15||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **tataś ca taṁ bhītaṁ matvā sa-kṛpamāha—yatheti | etadaparādha-bījena punastu pūrvavanmahad-aparādho na janayiṣyata ity arthaḥ ||15||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **abhiśāpāntaram eva, “aho kiṁ niraparādho hari-bhaktaḥ śaptaḥ” iti paścāttāpavatī prāha—he putreti | mātā yathā durnayaṁ putraṁ sva-hastena praharati prakṛtyaiva punaḥ snihyati, tathaiva tvām aham adaṇḍayam iti bhāvaḥ | ata eva mātṛ-samucitam evāha—bhūya iti | bālya-krīḍā-cāpalyena para-gṛha-vipriya-kāriṇaṁ śiśuṁ prahṛtya mātā yathā brūte—"he adānta ! punar evaṁ na kariṣyasi" iti tadvad evety arthaḥ | ata eva bhavānyāḥ so’bhiśāpaś citraketuṁ nāpacakāra, pratyuta vṛtra-janmani premā vṛddhim eva prāpa | satyāṁ prema-sampattau bhaktānāṁ pārṣada-tanutva-daitya-tanutvayor aviśeṣa-mananāt ||15||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.16 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**evaṁ śaptaś citraketur vimānād avaruhya saḥ |**

**prasādayām āsa satīṁ mūrdhnā namreṇa bhārata ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.17 ||**

**citraketur uvāca—**

**pratigṛhṇāmi te śāpam ātmano’ñjalināmbike |**

**devair martyāya yat proktaṁ pūrva-diṣṭaṁ hi tasya tat ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **pūrva-diṣṭaṁ prācīna-karma-prāptam eva ||17||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **pūrva-diṣṭaṁ hīti pūrvādiṣṭenaiva hi mamaiṣā buddhirjāteti | nanu, kevala-guṇa-hetutve cetanaṁ kartāraṁ vinā bandha-mokṣādikaṁ jīvānāṁ na syāt ? tatrāha—eka iti |_|_17||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **pratigṛhṇāmīti mamānena śāpena kāpi kṣatir na bhaviṣyati mahādeve tvayy apy akṛtāparādhatvād iti bhāvaḥ | nirāgaskāya mahyaṁ śaptavatyās tavāpi nātra ko’pi doṣa ity āha—devair iti | pūrva-diṣṭaṁ prācīna-karma-prāptam iti, bhaktasya tasya svasmiṁs tathā bhāvanā dainyena samucitaiva, vastutas tu jāta-premṇas tasya kutaḥ karma-gandho’pi prema-pūrva-daśāyām eva, kṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi mayi dṛṣṭe’khilātmani [bhā.pu. 11.20.30] ity-ādinā sarva-karma-kṣayokteḥ | harer bhakta-vaśyatva-prasiddhir bhaktānāṁ karmādhīnatve sati na siddhyet, na hi svayaṁ karmādhīno bhagavantam adhīnamāyaṁ vaśīkuryād iti | tataś ca tasya śāpānugraha-svargāpavarga-narakādi-sama-darśitva-mahā-bala-khyāpanārthaṁ vidyādharādhipatya-kupathya-dūrīkaraṇārthaṁ sva-virahoṣmaṇā prema-kṣud-vivardhanārthaṁ svīya-vaikuṇṭhāgata-sva-caraṇa-sākṣāt-sevā-mahā-mādhurya-bhoga-pradānārthaṁ ca svenaivāntaḥ-preritayā devyābhiśāpaḥ śrī-saṅkarṣaṇa-devenaiva bhagavatā snehavatā pitreva kārita iti tattvaṁ tat-tat-phala-darśanād avagatam ||17||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.18 ||**

**saṁsāra-cakra etasmin jantur ajñāna-mohitaḥ |**

**bhrāmyan sukhaṁ ca duḥkhaṁ ca bhuṅkte sarvatra sarvadā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ayaṁ ca saṁsāra-cakra-svabhāva eva na citram ity āha—saṁsāra-cakra iti ||18||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ayaṁ ca saṁsāra-cakraḥ svabhāva eva na citram ity āha—saṁsāreti ||18||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.19 ||**

**naivātmā na paraś cāpi kartā syāt sukha-duḥkhayoḥ |**

**kartāraṁ manyate’prājña ātmānaṁ param eva ca ||**

**madhvaḥ : **yat tad bhagavatā kḷptaṁ tad eva niyataṁ bhavet ||19||

**śrīdharaḥ : **ata evātra mama ca tava ca na ko’pi doṣa ity āha—naiveti ||19||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **aprājño’vivekī ||19||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.20 ||**

**guṇa-pravāha etasmin kaḥ śāpaḥ ko nv anugrahaḥ |**

**kaḥ svargo narakaḥ ko vā kiṁ sukhaṁ duḥkham eva vā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **evaṁ tāvat sukha-duḥkhādikam aṅgī-kṛtyoktam | idānīṁ tad api vastuto nāstīty āha—guṇānāṁ māyā-mayānāṁ pravāhe saṁsāre ||20||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **evaṁ tāvat sukha-duḥkhādikam aṅgī-kṛtyoktam | idānīṁ tu lavaṇākare patitaḥ sarvo lavaṇa-rasa iva saṁsāre sarva eva padārthaḥ saṁsāra iti sukha-duḥkhādi-bhedāvagamo nopapadyate ity āha—guṇa-pravāha iti | na hy atala-sparśa-pravāha-madhye patitasya yāvat taṭān avāptiḥ, tāvat kim api vastutaḥ sukhāyety ataḥ śāpānugrahādikaṁ sarvam api duḥkham eveti bhāvaḥ ||20||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.21 ||**

**ekaḥ sṛjati bhūtāni bhagavān ātma-māyayā |**

**eṣāṁ bandhaṁ ca mokṣaṁ ca sukhaṁ duḥkhaṁ ca niṣkalaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu māyā-guṇānāṁ ced ayaṁ pravāhas tarhi teṣāṁ jaḍatvād bandha-mokṣādy-anubhavo na syāt tatrāha—ekaḥ parameśvaro māyayā nimitta-bhūtayā bhūtāni prāṇinaḥ sṛjati | eṣāṁ bandhādikaṁ ca sṛjati | niṣkalaḥ svayaṁ bandhādi-śūnyaḥ ||21||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nanu tarhy atra guṇa-pravāhe ko vā pātayitā ko vāsmād uddharteti ced bhagavān evety āha—eka iti | ātma-māyayā rajasā sṛjati, sattvena pālayati, tamasā saṁharati | eṣāṁ bandhaṁ cāvidyayā mokṣaṁ ca sattvena sukhaṁ tamasā duḥkhaṁ ca | niṣkalaḥ kalā māyā, tad-rahitaḥ ||21||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.22 ||**

**na tasya kaścid dayitaḥ pratīpo**

**na jñāti-bandhur na paro na ca svaḥ |**

**samasya sarvatra nirañjanasya**

**sukhe na rāgaḥ kuta eva roṣaḥ ||**

**madhvaḥ : **sevāyogyātirekeṇa sva-nāmai na dāsyati |


    aparādhātirekeṇa nānyasyātaḥ samo hariḥ || iti māhātmye ||22||

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanv evaṁ-bhūta-viṣama-sṛṣṭau tasya kiṁ kāraṇam, priyādi-vaiṣamyābhāvād ity āśaṅkya yady api priyādayo na santi tathāpi tat tat karma-vaśāt sarvaṁ ghaṭata ity āha—na tasyeti dvābhyām | pratīpo’priyaḥ | na jñātir bandhuś cety arthaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—sarvatra samasya | tat kutaḥ ? nirañjanasya niḥsaṅgasya | ata eva tan-nimitte sukhe rāgo nāsti, rāgānubandhī roṣaḥ kutaḥ syāt ? ||22||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nanu tasya kaścit priyo’priyaś ca jīvo’vaśyaṁ vartata eva, yataḥ kim api badhnāti, kam api mocayati, kam api sukhayatīty āha—neti | na jñātir bandhuḥ, tatra hetuḥ—sarvatra samasya | samatve hetuḥ—nirañjanasya añjanaṁ māyā, tad-rahitasya | ata eva sukhe viṣaya-sukhe rāga āsaktir nāsti, viṣaya-sukha-prātikūlye roṣo dveṣaḥ kutaḥ syāt ? tad uktam—


    indriyasyendriyasyārthe rāga-dveṣau vyavasthitau |


    tayor na vaśam āgacchet tau hy asya paripanthinau || [gītā 3.34] iti |

tata eva rāga-dveṣa-mūlakau dayita-pratīpau tasya na sta iti bhāvaḥ ||22||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.23 ||**

**tathāpi tac-chakti-visarga eṣāṁ**

**sukhāya duḥkhāya hitāhitāya |**

**bandhāya mokṣāya ca mṛtyu-janmanoḥ**

**śarīriṇāṁ saṁsṛtaye’vakalpate ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yady apy eva tatrāpi tasya śaktyā māyayā yo visargaḥ puṇya-pāpādi-lakṣaṇaṁ karma eṣāṁ śarīriṇāṁ sukhādy-artham avakalpate samartho bhavati | yathoktaṁ gītāsu—bhūta-bhāvodbhava-karo visargaḥ karma-saṁjñitaḥ [gītā 8.3] iti |

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **evaṁ tasya sāmyaṁ cet, tarhi kathaṁ kam api sa sukhayati kam api duḥkhayati ? ity atrāha—tathāpīti | yadyapi sa sarvatra samaḥ, tad api tasya śaktyā māyayā yo visargaḥ anādi-puṇya-pāpādi-lakṣaṇa-karma-paramparā, sa eva sukhādy-artham avakalpate | ayam arthaḥ—yadyapi māyāyās tac-chaktitvāt sa eva sukha-duḥkhādikaṁ sṛjatīti tasya vaiṣamyam eva, tad api māyāyāḥ svarūpa-śaktitvābhāvāt sa na sukha-duḥkhādi sṛjatīti vastutas tasya sāmyam eva yathā māyika-viśvasya bhagavad-rūpatve’pi na bhagavat-svarūpa-bhūtatvam iti yathā sūrya-sambandhina ātapasya ghūka-kumudādīnāṁ duḥkhadatvena cakravāka-kamalādīnāṁ sukhadatvena vaiṣamye’pi sūryasya teṣu vaiṣamyaṁ ko’pi na varṇayati, tadvad iti bhāvaḥ ||23||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.24 ||**

**atha prasādaye na tvāṁ śāpa-mokṣāya bhāmini |**

**yan manyase hy asādhūktaṁ mama tat kṣamyatāṁ sati ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **atha tasmād bhāmini he kopane, tvāṁ kevalaṁ prasādayāmi na tu śāpa-mokṣāya | tarhi kiṁ prasādanenāta āha—mamoktam uktiṁ sādhv apy asādhuvan manyase, tat tvayā kṣamyatām ||24||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **yadyapi manyase anugṛhṇāsi, tat tadā mama asādhūktaṁ kṣamyatām |_|_24||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **atha ata eva tvāṁ kevalaṁ prasādayāmi, na tu śāpa-mokṣāya | he bhāmini ! avicāreṇa kopane ! nanu tarhi kiṁ prasādanena ? tatrāha—mayoktaṁ sādhv api yad asādhu manyase, tad asādhv evāstu, tvayā kṣamyatām | mama tu śāpe śāpānte vā duḥkha-sukhayor abhāvas tataḥ prasannāpi śāpāntaṁ mā kārṣīr iti bhāvaḥ ||24||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.25 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**iti prasādya giriśau citraketur arindama |**

**jagāma sva-vimānena paśyatoḥ smayatos tayoḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **giriśau bhavānī-śaṅkarau prasādya | smayator vismayaṁ kurvatoḥ satoḥ ||25||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **smayator vismayavatoḥ satoḥ ||25||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.26 ||**

**tatas tu bhagavān rudro rudrāṇīm idam abravīt |**

**devarṣi-daitya-siddhānāṁ pārṣadānāṁ ca śṛṇvatām ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.27 ||**

**śrī-rudra uvāca—**

**dṛṣṭavaty asi suśroṇi harer adbhuta-karmaṇaḥ |**

**māhātmyaṁ bhṛtya-bhṛtyānāṁ niḥspṛhāṇāṁ mahātmanām ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **dṛṣṭavatyasi bhavac-chāpe’pi bhayābhāvena tarkitavatyasi kim |_|_27||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he suśroṇi ! iti tvaṁ saundarya-guṇair evādhikya-māhātmyāsi, na tu bhakti-jñāna-vairāgyādibhir iti parihāso dhvanitaḥ | adbhuta-karmaṇa iti harer idam adbhutaṁ karma mayā dṛṣṭaṁ yat tvayā śāpaṁ dāpá tavāpakarṣa eva tena kṛtaḥ, sva-bhaktasya prema-sampadbhir īṣad api nyūnatām aprāṭasyāgaṇita-devī-śāpatva-rūpa-prabhāva-khyāpanayā paramotkarṣa eva kṛtaḥ | mahātmanām iti tayā kopa-bharitayāpi datto’bhiśāpas tasmai yadi khalv īṣad api duḥkhaṁ dātum apārayiṣyat, tadāpi te śāpaḥ saphalo’bhaviṣyat | hanta hanta vyartha evāyam abhūd ity ato mahātmasu premi-bhakteṣu tvayādyārabhya naivaṁ vyavahartavyam iti śikṣā dhvanitā ||27||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.28 ||**

**nārāyaṇa-parāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati |**

**svargāpavarga-narakeṣv api tulyārtha-darśinaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **svargādāv eva tulyo’rthaḥ prayojanam iti draṣṭuṁ śīlaṁ yeṣāṁ te tathā ||28||

**sanātanaḥ **(habhagavat-sandarbha.vi. 10.190) : kutaścana kasmāccid api devādeḥ śāpāder vā sakāśān na bhayaṁ prāpnuvanti | yataḥ svargādiṣv api tulyo’rthaḥ prayojanam iti draṣṭuṁ śīlaṁ yeṣāṁ te | tathā na cānyat kim api vāñchanty apīti bhāvaḥ ||28||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **śrī-nārāyaṇaṁ vinānyatra hānopādāna-dṛṣṭi-rāhityāpavarga iva svarga iva narake ’pi tulyam ekam evārthaṁ nārāyaṇa-rūpa-puruṣārthaṁ draṣṭum anubhavituṁ śīlaṁ yeṣāṁ te tulya-śabdasyaika-vācitvam, raṣābhyāṁ noṇaḥ samāna-padeitivat |_|_28||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nanv evaṁ māhātmyavattve bhaktānāṁ ko hetus tatra nārāyaṇaika-niṣṭhatvam eva nānya ity āha—nārāyaṇeti | na kevalam ete citraketu-prabhṛtaya eva, api tu sarva eva | svargeti trayāṇām eva bhakti-sukha-rāhityenārocakatvāviśeṣād iti bhāvaḥ ||28||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.29 ||**

**dehināṁ deha-saṁyogād dvandvānīśvara-līlayā |**

**sukhaṁ duḥkhaṁ mṛtir janma śāpo’nugraha eva ca ||**

**madhvaḥ : **ato’nyeṣāṁ varaḥ śāpo guṇa-doṣa-prakartṛtā |


    svataḥ prāptābheda-kṛtir vāsanā-rūpiṇo yathā ||


    vidyamānasya manasi punaḥ svapneṣu darśanam |


    bhagavad-vaśatā yasmāt sarveṣāṁ jñeyam eva tat || iti prakāśa-saṁhitāyām ||29-30||

**śrīdharaḥ : **tatra tad uktam eva hetum āha dvābhyām | dehināṁ sukhaṁ duḥkham ity-ādi-dvandvānīśvarasya līlayā māyayā bhavanti | teṣu ca guṇa-doṣa-vikalpaś cety anvayaḥ ||29||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nārāyaṇa-niṣṭhatvābhāve tv evaṁ bhaved ity āha—dehinām iti | īśvara-līlayeti tad-īkṣaṇa-līlā-labdha-valayā māyayety arthaḥ ||29||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.30 ||**

**aviveka-kṛtaḥ puṁso hy artha-bheda ivātmani |**

**guṇa-doṣa-vikalpaś ca bhid eva srajivat kṛtaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **iṣṭān iṣṭa-bheda iva yaḥ sphurati sa ātmany artha-bhedaḥ sukhādi-bhedaḥ puṁsaḥ svapne yathā aviveka-kṛto bhavati | sraji-vat sarpa-mālādibhir yathā tathaiva kṛta ity arthaḥ | srag-vad iti vaktavye sraji-vad ity ārṣam | pāṭhāntare tu sugamam ||30||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **aviveketyasya ṭīkāyāṁ te tu cetyadhyāhṛtam iṣṭāniṣṭeti | guṇa-doṣa-vikalpasya vyākhyeyaṁ bhidā yathetyatra bhidā ceti jñeyam |ca-kārānvayāttat-kṛta iti pāṭhāntaram |_|_30||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tasmān māyikam avāstavaṁ vastu sukha-duḥkhādikam asthiratvād avastv iva jānīyād ity āha—aviveketi | puṁsaḥ svapne ātmani artha-bhedaḥ kṣīra-bhojana-putra-maraṇādi iva jāgare’pi guṇa-doṣa-vikalpaḥ sukha-duḥkhādi-bheda-kṛto jñeyaḥ | tatra dṛṣṭāntaḥ—sraji mālāyāṁ bhit rajjur iyam iti sarpo’yam iti bheda eva, vat yathety arthaḥ | iva vad veti sādṛśya ity abhidhānāt | sraji tad iti pāṭhe sraji mālāyāṁ tattvato hetor bhidā bheda iva | prathame pāṭhe bhit kvib-antaḥ dvitīye bhidā ṭāvantaḥ ||30||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.31 ||**

**vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktim udvahatāṁ nṛṇām |**

**jñāna-vairāgya-vīryāṇāṁ na hi kaścid vyapāśrayaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ato bhāgavatānāṁ nispṛhatvam ucitam evety āha—vāsudeva iti | jñāna-vairāgyayor vīryaṁ balaṁ yeṣāṁ teṣām | vyapāśrayo viśiṣṭa-buddhyā āśrayaṇīyo’rtho nāsti ||31||

**sanātanaḥ **(habhagavat-sandarbha.vi. 11.581) : tad eva sarva-nairapekṣyeṇa draḍhayati—vāsudeva iti dvābhyām | jñāna-vairāgyayor vīryaṁ balaṁ yeṣām | tayor api vīryaṁ yebhya iti vā | vyapāśrayo viśiṣṭa-buddhyā āśrayaṇīyo’rtho nāsti ||31||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tad evaṁ jñānināṁ dvandveṣu jñānābhyāsenāpy avastu-buddhir duṣkarā | bhaktānāṁ tu jñāna-vairāgyayor bhakty-anubhāva-rūpatvāt vināpi jñānābhyāsena teṣv anusandhānam api na bhavatīty āha—vāsudeva iti |iha saṁsāre kaścid apy artho viśeṣasyākarṣasya cāśrayo nāsti | bhakty-anusandhānād eva māyika-vastūnām utkarṣāpakarṣānusandhānaṁ naiva jāyate iti bhaktānāṁ tat tam avadhārayeti bhāvaḥ ||31||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.32 ||**

**nāhaṁ viriñco na kumāra-nāradau**

**na brahma-putrā munayaḥ sureśāḥ |**

**vidāma yasyehitam aṁśakāṁśakā**

**na tat-svarūpaṁ pṛthag-īśa-māninaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **asya ca hari-dāsatvena tat svabhāvatvān naitac citram iti vaktuṁ harer māhātmyam āha—nāham iti dvābhyām | īhitam abhiprāyaṁ līlāṁ vā yadā vayaṁ na vidmas tadā tasya svarūpam aṁśakāṁśakā api santaḥ pṛthag-īśa-mānino na vidur eva ||32||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **pṛthag-īśa-māninaś cet tarhi vayam aṁśakāṁśakā api yasyehitaṁ svarūpaṁ ca na vidāma, kintu bhaktāś cet tarhi sarve’pi vidur ity arthaḥ |_|_32||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **asmad-ādīnām api tattvaṁ śṛṇv ity āha—nāham iti | īhitam abhiprāyaṁ līlāṁ vā na vidāma, yataḥ pṛthag-īśa-māninaḥ ||32||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.33 ||**

**na hy asyāsti priyaḥ kaścin nāpriyaḥ svaḥ paro’pi vā |**

**ātmatvāt sarva-bhūtānāṁ sarva-bhūta-priyo hariḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ata eva harir api sarveṣāṁ bhūtānāṁ priyaḥ ||33||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **bhakta-māhātmyam eva citraketu-dṛṣṭāntena spaṣṭayati—na hy asyeti dvābhyām | priyāpriyayoḥ sva-parayoś ca bhedo nāstīty arthaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—ātmatvād iti, ātmatvena sāmyād anapekṣaṇīyatvāc cety arthaḥ | ātmatvād eva hetoḥ sarva-bhūtānāṁ tu priyaḥ nirupādhika-prīti-viṣayaḥ |_|_33||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **hareś ca tattvaṁ śṛṇu—na hīti | sa tu hariḥ sarva-bhūtānāṁ priya eva, tad api yat sa keṣāñcit priyo na bhavati, keṣāñcid dveṣyaś ca na bhavati, tatra tāratamyena māyaiva kāraṇam iti tasmān māyāyāś ca tattvaṁ jñāpitam ||33||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.34-35 ||**

**tasya cāyaṁ mahā-bhāgaś citraketuḥ priyo’nugaḥ |**

**sarvatra sama-dṛk śānto hy ahaṁ caivācyuta-priyaḥ ||**

**tasmān na vismayaḥ kāryaḥ puruṣeṣu mahātmasu |**

**mahāpuruṣa-bhakteṣu śānteṣu sama-darśiṣu ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ahaṁ caivācyutasya priyaḥ, tasmān mamāsmin droho nābhūd iti bhāvaḥ ||34-35||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **viruddham, ata evāgre vakṣyate—itihāsam imaṁ puṇyaṁ citraketor mahātmanaḥ [bhā.pu. 6.17.40] iti |_|_35||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kintv asya citraketor mama ca tattvaṁ śṛṇv ity āha—tasya sarvatra samasyāpi |


    samo’haṁ sarva-bhūteṣu na me dveṣyo’sti na priyaḥ |


    ye bhajanti tu māṁ bhaktyā mayi te teṣu cāpy aham ||[gītā 9.29]

iti tad-vākyād evāyam anugaś citraketuḥ priyaḥ | mamāpi bhaktatvād ahaṁ ca priyaḥ, tasmād āvayoḥ saṅkarṣaṇa-bhaktayoḥ paraspara-sakhyenāntaḥ-snehavattvāt kaṭhorokty-ādikam api sakhya-sukha-poṣakam eva, tvaṁ tu vṛthaiva kopiny abhūḥ | 

kiṁ ca, satyam aham īdṛśī eva, tvaṁ tv ātmānaṁ niṣkiñcanam aikāntika-bhaktatvena sarvatra darśayasi | atha ca rahasi vidyādharī-sahasreṇa saha ramase, tasmāt tvaṁ kapaṭī, ahaṁ tv ātmānaṁ strī-lāmpaṭya-mayaṁ darśayan niṣkapaṭa evāsmi | 

kiṁ ca, tvaṁ bhaktiṁ darśayasi, viṣaya-bhogaṁ gopayasi | ahaṁ tu tad-viparīta eva varte ity āvayor antaram ete sabhyā eva sākṣitvenācakṣatām ity-ādi-narma-goṣṭhī-rasāsvādo’py adyābhaviṣyad eva | yadi tvam antarā antarāyaṁ nākariṣya iti tvat-kopa-vairasyād eva sa nābhūd ity upālambho dhvanitaḥ | hanta hanta ! kṣatra-bandhuṣv arvācīneṣv adhunaiva bhakti-mārgam ārūḍheṣu taveśvarasyānādi-mahā-bhaktasyāpy etādṛśeṣv apy etāvān bhāvo namas tubhyaṁ tad iti vismayavatyāṁ tasyāṁ satyam etāvān eva bhāva ity āha—tasmād iti ||34-35||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.36 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**iti śrutvā bhagavataḥ śivasyomābhibhāṣitam |**

**babhūva śānta-dhī rājan devī vigata-vismayā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śānta-dhīr iti svīya-pūrva-svabhāva-smṛtyā lajjayā paṭāñcalena mukham āccādvayāmāseti bhāvaḥ ||36||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.37 ||**

**iti bhāgavato devyāḥ pratiśaptum alantamaḥ |**

**mūrdhnā sa jagṛhe śāpam etāvat sādhu-lakṣaṇam ||**

**madhvaḥ : **devā eva tad anyebhyaḥ śaktā nāsty atra saṁśayaḥ |


    aśaktā api śaktānāṁ śaktāḥ śāpādiṣu sphuṭam ||


    tathāpy aśaktair vihitāḥ śāpādy-aśaktimatsu vai |


    atyalpāś cālpa-kālāś ca na samyak prabhavanti ca ||


    yatnenāpohitaṁ śaktyā uttamais tu na saṁśayaḥ |


    uttameṣu kṛtāḥ śāpāḥ kartṝṇāṁ jñāna-puṇyayoḥ ||


    niḥśeṣeṇa nihantāras tad-anugraham antarā |


    sadārayor brahma-viṣṇau vara-śāpādayo’khilāḥ ||


    tad anyena kṛtāḥ sarve niṣphalā eva niścayāt |


    na cāpy avāstavāḥ śāpābhavanty eṣāṁ tu kutracit ||


    vara-viṣṇoḥ śriyaś ca syur brahmaṇaś ca yathā-kramam |


    uttamair adhamānāṁ tu varāḥ śāpā yathoditam |


    sampūrṇa-phaladā eva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || iti skānde ||37||

**śrīdharaḥ : **pratiśāpaṁ dātum alan-tamaḥ samartha-tamo’pi ||37||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **citraketur arvācīnatvād alpa-prabhāva iti mā maṁsthā ity āha—itīti | devyā devyai alaṁ tama atisamartho’pi ||37||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.38 ||**

**jajñe tvaṣṭur dakṣiṇāgnau dānavīṁ yonim āśritaḥ |**

**vṛtra ity abhivikhyāto jñāna-vijñāna-saṁyutaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yoniṁ jātim ||38||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.39 ||**

**etat te sarvam ākhyātaṁ yan māṁ tvaṁ paripṛcchasi |**

**vṛtrasyāsura-jāteś ca kāraṇaṁ bhagavan-mateḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **asura-jāter asura-bhāvenotpatteḥ | bhagavati mateś ca ||39||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **asurajāteḥ kāraṇaṁ mahadaparādhaḥ bhagavanmateḥ kāraṇaṁ mahadanugrahaḥ |_|_39||

**viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.17.40-41 ||**

**itihāsam imaṁ puṇyaṁ citraketor mahātmanaḥ |**

**māhātmyaṁ viṣṇu-bhaktānāṁ śrutvā bandhād vimucyate ||**

**ya etat prātar utthāya śraddhayā vāg-yataḥ paṭhet |**

**itihāsaṁ hariṁ smṛtvā sa yāti paramāṁ gatim ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **etad etam ||41||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

 —o)0(o—

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ṣaṣṭhasya saptadaśo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

—o)0(o—

iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ ṣaṣṭha-skandhe

citraketūpākhyāne

saptadaśo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 6.17 ||



(6.18)


### athāṣṭadaśo’dhyāyaḥ


## marud-utpattir nāma 

**|| 6.18.1 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**pṛśnis tu patnī savituḥ sāvitrīṁ vyāhṛtiṁ trayīm |**

**agnihotraṁ paśuṁ somaṁ cāturmāsyaṁ mahā-makhān ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **

ādityānāṁ caturthasya tvaṣṭur vaṁśa-prasaṅgataḥ|

proktam indra-kṛtaṁ viśva- rūpa-vṛtra-vadhādikam ||

aditeḥ pañcamādīnaṁ putrāṇām anvayoktibhiḥ |

aṣṭādaśe diter garbhe śakreṇa marutāṁ bhidā ||

tvaṣṭur vaṁśam anukramya sa-prasaṅgaṁ yathākramam |

ādityānām athānyeṣāṁ vaṁśān āha munīśvaraḥ ||

dakṣa-kanyānvayānukathane adityā dvādaśa putrāḥ proktāḥ—


    vivasvān aryamā pūṣā tvaṣṭā’tha savitā bhagaḥ | 


    dhātā vidhātā varuṇo mitraḥ śakra urukramaḥ || iti | 

tatra ṣaṣṭhādhyāyān tam ārabhya viśvarūpa-vṛtra-citraketūpākhyānais tvaṣṭur vaṁśam anuvarṇyedānīṁ savitur vaṁśam āha—pṛśnis tv ati | sāvitrīm ity-ādiṣu prāsūtety uttarasyānuṣaṅgaḥ | paśuṁ paśu-yāgam | mahā-makhān pañca-yajñān ||1||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **pṛśnis tv iti trikam ||1||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **

aṣṭādaśe hata-sutā ditiḥ kṛtvā vrataṁ dadhau |

yaṁ tasmāc chatru-sañchinnād garbhāj jajñe marud-gaṇaḥ ||

turyasyāditi-putrāṇāṁ tvaṣṭur anvaya-kīrtanaiḥ |

prasaṅgataḥ samāyātāḥ viśvarūpa-vadhādikam ||

citraketv-abhiśāpāntāṁ samāpyaiva kathā-sudhām |

aditeḥ pañcamādīnāṁ sutānāṁ vaṁca ucyate ||

paśuṁ paśu-yāgaṁ mahā-makhān pañca-yajñān ||1||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.2 ||**

**siddhir bhagasya bhāryāṅga mahimānaṁ vibhuṁ prabhum |**

**āśiṣaṁ ca varārohāṁ kanyāṁ prāsūta suvratām ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.3 ||**

**dhātuḥ kuhūḥ sinīvālī rākā cānumatis tathā |**

**sāyaṁ darśam atha prātaḥ pūrṇamāsam anukramāt ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **dhātur bhāryā kuhūḥ sāyaṁ putraṁ prāsūta | evaṁ sinīvālī darśam ity anukramāt ||3||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.4 ||**

**agnīn purīṣyān ādhatta kriyāyāṁ samanantaraḥ |**

**carṣaṇī varuṇasyāsīd yasyāṁ jāto bhṛguḥ punaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **samanantaro vidhātā kriyāyāṁ bhāryāyāṁ purīṣyān agnīn pañca citān,purīṣyāso agnayaḥ iti,pañca vā ete’gnayo yac cittayaḥiti śruteḥ | carṣaṇī varuṇasya bhāryāsīt | pūrvaṁ brahmaṇaḥ putro bhṛgur yasyāṁ punar jātaḥ ||4||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **agnīnityarddhakam |

**viśvanāthaḥ : **samanataro vidhātā kriyāyāṁ bhāryāyāṁ purīṣyan purīṣya-saṁjñān agnīn, pañca-citīḥ purīṣyāso’gnayaḥ iti śruteḥ | carṣaṇī varuṇasya bhāryāsīt | punar iti prāg brahma-putro’pipunar varuṇa-putro’bhūt ||4||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.5 ||**

**vālmīkiś ca mahā-yogī valmīkād abhavat kila |**

**agastyaś ca vasiṣṭhaś ca mitrā-varuṇayor ṛṣī ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **vālmīkir varuṇasyaiva putro’bhavat | etau varuṇasyāsādhāraṇau putrau | tathotsargādayo’pi mitrasyāsādhāraṇāḥ | tayor eva sādhāraṇau dvau putrāv āha | agastyaś ca vasiṣṭhaś ca ṛṣī mitrā-varuṇayor abhavatām ||5||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhṛgu-vālmīkī varuṇasyāsādhāraṇau putrau | tathotsargādayomitrasyāsādhāraṇāḥ putrā vakṣyante | tayor mitrā-varuṇayoḥ sādhāraṇau dvau putraucāha | agastyaś ca vasiṣṭhaś caitau ṛṣī mitrā-varuṇayor abhavatām ||5||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.6 ||**

**retaḥ siṣicatuḥ kumbhe urvaśyāḥ sannidhau drutam |**

**revatyāṁ mitra utsargam ariṣṭaṁ pippalaṁ vyadhāt ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yata ubhāv api kumbhe retaḥ siṣicatuḥ,satre ha jātāviṣitā namobhiḥ kumbhe retaḥ siṣicatuḥ samānam [ṛ.ve. 7.33.24] iti śruteḥ | drutaṁ skannam ||6||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yato reta ity-ādi,kumbhe retaḥ siṣicatuḥ samānam [ṛ.ve. 7.33.24] iti śruteḥ | drutaṁ skannam ||6||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.7 ||**

**paulomyām indra ādhatta trīn putrān iti naḥ śrutam |**

**jayantam ṛṣabhaṁ tāta tṛtīyaṁ mīḍhuṣaṁ prabhuḥ ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.8 ||**

**urukramasya devasya māyā-vāmana-rūpiṇaḥ |**

**kīrtau patnyāṁ bṛhacchlokas tasyāsan saubhagādayaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **māyayā svarūpa-śaktyā vāmana-rūpavataḥ svarūpa-bhūtayā nitya-śaktyā māyākhyayā yutaḥ | ato māyā-mayaṁ viṣṇuṁ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ iti mādhva-bhāṣya-pramāṇita-śruteḥ ||8||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.9 ||**

**tat-karma-guṇa-vīryāṇi kāśyapasya mahātmanaḥ |**

**paścād vakṣyāmahe’dityāṁ yathaivāvatatāra ha ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : **paścād aṣṭama-skandhe ||9||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.10 ||**

**atha kaśyapa-dāyādān daiteyān kīrtayāmi te |**

**yatra bhāgavataḥ śrīmān prahrādo balir eva ca ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **atheti | kaśyapasyāditeḥ putrāṇāṁ dvādaśādityānāṁ santatim uktvā, diteḥ putrān kathayāmīty arthaḥ ||10||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **atheti kathāntarārambhe dāyādān putrān daiteyān dityāṁ jātān ||10||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.11 ||**

**diter dvāv eva dāyādau daitya-dānava-vanditau |**

**hiraṇyakaśipur nāma hiraṇyākṣaś ca kīrtitau ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **hiraṇyakaśipur hiraṇyākṣaś cetiprathamaṁ dvāv eva | tau ca kīrtitau tṛtīya-skandhe ||11||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.12 ||**

**hiraṇyakaśipor bhāryā kayādhur nāma dānavī |**

**jambhasya tanayā sā tu suṣuve caturaḥ sutān ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.13 ||**

**saṁhrādaṁ prāg anuhrādaṁ hrādaṁ prahrādam eva ca |**

**tat-svasā siṁhikā nāma rāhuṁ vipracito’grahīt ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **vipracito dānavād bhartuḥ sakāśād rāhuḥ putram agrahīt ||13||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **vipracito dānavād patyuḥ sakāśād rāhuḥ putram agrahīt prāpa ||13||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.14 ||**

**śiro’harad yasya hariś cakreṇa pibato’mṛtam |**

**saṁhrādasya kṛtir bhāryā- sūta pañcajanaṁ tataḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tataḥ saṁhrādād asūta ||14||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.15 ||**

**hrādasya dhamanir bhāryā- sūta vātāpim ilvalam |**

**yo’gastyāya tv atithaye pece vātāpim ilvalaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **yo meṣa-rūpaṁ vātāpiṁ pece tam ilvalam | yaṁ pece taṁ vātāpiṁ cāsūtety anvayaḥ ||15||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ya ilvalo’gastyāya | agastyaṁ bhojayituṁ vātāpiṁ meṣa-rūpaṁ pece ||15||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.16 ||**

**anuhrādasya sūryāyāṁ bāṣkalo mahiṣas tathā |**

**virocanas tu prāhrādir devyāṁ tasyābhavad baliḥ ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.17 ||**

**bāṇa-jyeṣṭhaṁ putra-śatam aśanāyāṁ tato’bhavat |**

**tasyānubhāvaṁ suślokyaṁ paścād evābhidhāsyate ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tato baleḥ sakāśād abhavat tasya baler anubhāvaḥ suślokyaḥ puṇya-kīrty-arhaḥ | yad vā, , anubhāvyate sadbhiḥ stūyata ity anubhāvam | suślokyaṁ yaśa iti śeṣaḥ ||17||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tasya baleḥ anubhāvam ity ārṣam, bāhya-karma sambandhena vā ||17||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.18 ||**

**bāṇa ārādhya giriśaṁ lebhe tad-gaṇa-mukhyatām |**

**yat-pārśve bhagavān āste hy adyāpi pura-pālakaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tasya gaṇeṣu mukhyatāṁ prādhānyam ||18||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.19 ||**

**marutaś ca diteḥ putrāś catvāriṁśan navādhikāḥ |**

**ta āsann aprajāḥ sarve nītā indreṇa sātmatām ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **sātmatāṁ samāna-rūpatām ||19||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sātmatāṁ samāna-svabhāvatām devatvaṁ prāpitā ity arthaḥ ||19||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.20 ||**

**śrī-rājovāca—**

**kathaṁ ta āsuraṁ bhāvam apohyautpattikaṁ guro |**

**indreṇa prāpitāḥ sātmyaṁ kiṁ tat sādhu kṛtaṁ hi taiḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **sātmyaṁ devatvaṁ prāpitāḥ ||20||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **apohya tyājayitvā ||20||

**viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.21 ||**

**ime śraddadhate brahmann ṛṣayo hi mayā saha |**

**parijñānāya bhagavaṁs tan no vyākhyātum arhasi ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **nanu kathaṁ bhavānimāṁ bahiraṅgāṁ kathāṁ śuśrūṣate ? tatrāha—ime śraddadhata iti | mayā saheti svasya gauṇatvaṁ bodhayaṁstathaiva vyañjitavān ||21||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ime munayaḥ śraddadhata iti svasyaiva śraddhāṁ muniṣv āropayati | rahasyam arthaṁ tān jñāpayitum ||21||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.22 ||**

**śrī-sūta uvāca—**

**tad viṣṇurātasya sa bādarāyaṇir**

**vaco niśamyādṛtam alpam arthavat |**

**sabhājayan san nibhṛtena cetasā**

**jagāda satrāyaṇa sarva-darśanaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ādṛtaṁ sādaram | alpaṁ mitākṣaram | arthavat bahv-artha-yuktam | satramayanam āśrayo yasya he satrāyaṇa śaunaka ||22||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **ata eva ślāghate—taditi | ādṛtam ṛṣīṇāmādareṇa sahitam arthavat etacca bhagavad-ārādhana-viśeṣa-sambandhenaiva bhavediti svābhīṣṭa-yuktaṁ sannibhṛtena śrī-bhagavat-sukha-pūrveṇa atastadapi bhagavat-sambandhaṁ yojayiṣyatīti bhāvaḥ | ṭīkāyāṁ bahv-artham iti ṛṣy-abhipreta-śrī-śukābhipreta-siddhi-yuktam ||22||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **arthavadanekārtha-yuktam | tatraiko jijñāsito’rtho’smād upākhyānāl labhyate | yathā para-hiṁsām abhisandhāyāpi tāmasīṁ bhagavad-bhaktiṁ kurvann aśuddha-citto’pi niścalām atāmasīṁ bhaktim ānuṣaṅgikīṁ saṁsārān muktiṁ citta-śuddhiṁ prāptyā para-jighāṁsā-nivṛttiṁ ca labhata ity atra ditir eva pramāṇaṁ, tathā kuṭila-cittā vivekino’pi yān doṣān pareṣāṁ paśyanti, tān eva doṣān svasmin sthitān api na paśyanti ity atra kṛmi-viḍ ity-ādika-vacanāt ditir eva pramāṇam iti dvitīyaḥ | strī-māyayā mahā-vijño’pi pratāryo bhavatīty atra kaśyapa eva pramāṇam iti tṛtīyaḥ | alpaṁ mitākṣaraṁ sannibhṛtena sampūrṇena ekāgrīkṛtenety arthaḥ | he satrāyaṇa śaunaka ||22||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.23 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**hata-putrā ditiḥ śakra-pārṣṇi-grāheṇa viṣṇunā |**

**manyunā śoka-dīptena jvalantī paryacintayat ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **śakrasya pārṣṇi-grāheṇa pṛṣṭhataḥ sahāyena ||23||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śakrasya pārṣṇi-grāheṇa pṛṣṭhataḥ sahāyena, parokṣa-sāhāyya-kartrety arthaḥ ||23||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.24 ||**

**kadā nu bhrātṛ-hantāram indriyārāmam ulbaṇam |**

**aklinna-hṛdayaṁ pāpaṁ ghātayitvā śaye sukham ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **bhrātṛ-hantāram indraṁ mārayitvā sukhinī kadā syām iti cintayām āsa ditiḥ | ulbaṇaṁ krūram | aklinna-hṛdayaṁ kaṭhina-cittam ||24||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ulbaṇaṁ krūram | sukhaṁ śaye sukhena nidrāmīty arthaḥ ||24||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.25 ||**

**kṛmi-viḍ-bhasma-saṁjñāsīd yasyeśābhihitasya ca |**

**bhūta-dhruk tat-kṛte svārthaṁ kiṁ veda nirayo yataḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu rājā sva-deha-rakṣārthamanyeṣāṁ ghātaṁ karoty eva kim atra citraṁ tatrāha—kṛmīti | **īśaḥ** prabhur ity **abhihitasyāpiyasya** pūrveṣāṁ rājñāṁ dehasya maraṇānantaraṁ dvi-tri-dināvasthitasya **kṛmaya** iti, śvādibhir bhakṣitasya tu **viṣṭheti**, dagdhasya **bhasmeti** ca **saṁjñā** āsīt | **tat-kṛte** tasya dehasyārthe yo bhūtebhyo druhyati, sa **kiṁ svārthaṁ veda** ? na vedaiva | tatra hetuḥ—**yato** bhūta-drohān **nirayo** bhavati ||25||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **īśābhihatasya īśo rājety-abhihitasyāpi dehasya maraṇānantaraṁ dvi-tri-dināvasthitatve kṛmaya iti, śvādibhir bhakṣitatve viṣṭheti, putrādibhir dagdhatve bhasmeti saṁjñāsīt | pūrva-pūrva-nṛpāṇām api tathā dṛṣṭatvād iti bhūta-nirdeśaḥ | tasya dehasya kṛte yo bhūtebhyo druhyati, sa kiṁ svārthaṁ veda ?naiva, yataḥ svasyaiva nirayo bhavati | tasmād indra eva viveka-śūnya iti vyañjayati | atha ca, svayam eva viveka-śūnyā, yata indraṁ jighāṁsuḥ, svayam apīndram eva bhūta-druhaṁ, svayam aklinna-hṛdayāpīndram evāklinna-hṛdayaṁ, svayaṁ svārthānabhijñāpi indram eva svārthānabhijñaṁ manyata | ity ato viveko’py avivekinām avivekam eva dṛḍhayatīti darśitam ||25||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.26 ||**

**āśāsānasya tasyedaṁ dhruvam unnaddha-cetasaḥ |**

**mada-śoṣaka indrasya bhūyād yena suto hi me ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : idaṁ** dehādikaṁ **dhruvaṁ** nityam **āśāsānasya** manyamānasya, ata **unnaddham** ucchṛṅkhalaṁ **ceto** yasya, **tasyendrasya** yo **madaḥ**, tasya **śoṣakaḥ putro** me yena hetunā **bhūyād** bhavet ||26||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **āśāsānasyeti yena bhavet, tat tu bhartṛ-priyācaraṇam eveti bhāvenety arthaḥ ||26||

**viśvanāthaḥ : yenaiva** tena duśceṣṭitena hetunaiva tasya **mada-śoṣakaḥ suto me bhūyād** iti me prārthanety arthaḥ | tasya katham-bhūtasya ? idaṁ dehādikaṁ dhruvaṁ nityam **āśāsānasya** manyamānasya **ucchṛṅkhala-cetasaḥ** ||26||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.27-28 ||**

**iti bhāvena sā bhartur ācacārāsakṛt priyam |**

**śuśrūṣayānurāgeṇa praśrayeṇa damena ca ||**

**bhaktyā paramayā rājan manojñair valgu-bhāṣitaiḥ |**
