**mano jagrāha bhāva-jñā sa-smitāpāṅga-vīkṣaṇaiḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **bhartuḥ priyācaraṇam eveti bhāvena sā bhartuḥ priyam asakṛd ācacāra||27||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhartari tuṣyati strīṇāṁ manorathaḥ siddhyati, tasmād ahaṁ paricaryayā patiṁ toṣayāmīti bhāvena ||27||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.29 ||**

**evaṁ striyā jaḍī-bhūto vidvān api manojñayā**[^23]** |**

**bāḍham ity āha vivaśo na tac citraṁ hi yoṣiti ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **vivaśaḥ strī-paratantraḥ san bāḍhaṁ tava manorathaṁ pūrayiṣyāmīti yadāha, tan na citram ||29||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bāḍhaṁ tava mano-rathaṁ pūrayiṣyāmīti yadāha, tan na citram ||29||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.30 ||**

**vilokyaikānta-bhūtāni bhūtāny ādau prajāpatiḥ |**

**striyaṁ cakre sva-dehārdhaṁ yayā puṁsāṁ matir hṛtā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tatra hetum āha—vilokyeti | ekānta-bhūtāni niḥsaṅgāni maithunena sṛṣṭi-vṛddhy-arthaṁ sva-dehārdham eva striyaṁ cakre ||30||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : ekānta-bhūtāni** niḥsaṅgāni | **matir hṛtā**, ata eva saṁsāra-pravāho ’vicchinno ’bhūd iti bhāvaḥ ||30||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.31 ||**

**evaṁ śuśrūṣitas tāta bhagavān kaśyapaḥ striyā |**

**prahasya parama-prīto ditim āhābhinandya ca ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **evaṁ striyā śuśrūṣitaḥ san ||31||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.32 ||**

**śrī-kaśyapa uvāca—**

**varaṁ varaya vāmoru prītas te’ham anindite |**

**striyā bhartari suprīte kaḥ kāma iha cāgamaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **iha ca-kārāt paratra ca | agamo’prāpyaḥ ||32||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **agamo’prāpyaḥ ||32||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.33-34 ||**

**patir eva hi nārīṇāṁ daivataṁ paramaṁ smṛtam |**

**mānasaḥ sarva-bhūtānāṁ vāsudevaḥ śriyaḥ patiḥ ||**

**sa eva devatā-liṅgair nāma-rūpa-vikalpitaiḥ |**

**ijyate bhagavān pumbhiḥ strībhiś ca pati-rūpa-dhṛk ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nanu parameśvare suprīte sarva-kāma-prāptir iti prasiddhaṁ | tatrāha—patir eveti | nanu manasi sthitaḥ śrī-vāsudeva eva lakṣmī-patiḥ paraṁ daivatam iti prasiddham ? satyam, sa eva svādhikāreṇa rūpa-bhedaiḥ pūjyata ity āha—mānasa iti sārdhena |devatā-liṅgair mūrtibhir upalakṣitaḥ | tāny evāha—nāma indrādi, rūpaṁ vajra-hastatvādi, tābhyāṁ vividhaṁ kalpitaiḥ ||33-34||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **patiḥ khalv atra jīva eva | sa kathaṁ paraṁ daivatam īśvaraḥ syāt ? tatrāha—mānasaḥ manasaś cittasyādhiṣṭhātā yo vāsudevaḥ, sa eva bhagavān devatānāṁ liṅgaiś cihnair ijyate | kīdṛśaiḥ ? nāma indrādi-rūpaṁ vajra-hastatvādi, tābhyām vividhaṁ kalpitaiḥ, indrāya svāhā, agnaye svāhā ity-ādibhir nāma-rūpa-bhedena pumbhiḥ karmi-lokair bhagavān eva ijyate yathā, tathā strībhiḥ pati-rūpeṇety arthaḥ ||33-34||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.35-36 ||**

**tasmāt pati-vratā nāryaḥ śreyas-kāmāḥ sumadhyame |**

**yajante’nanya-bhāvena patim ātmānam īśvaram ||**

**so’haṁ tvayārcito bhadre īdṛg-bhāvena bhaktitaḥ |**

**taṁ te sampādaye kāmam asatīnāṁ sudurlabham ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.37 ||**

**ditir uvāca—**

**varado yadi me brahman putram indra-haṇaṁ vṛṇe |**

**amṛtyuṁ mṛta-putrāhaṁ yena me ghātitau sutau ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **indra-haṇam indra-hantāram | amṛtyuṁ mṛtyu-śūnyam | yenendreṇa viṣṇunā sahāyena ghātitau ||37||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **indra-haṇam indra-hantāram | hanter gaty-arthatvāt pakṣe, indrānugam | amṛtyuṁ sarvair avadhyam | pakṣe, devatvād amaram | ūnapañcāśadbhir eka eva devo māruta ity eka-vacanam ||37||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.38 ||**

**niśamya tad-vaco vipro vimanāḥ paryatapyata |**

**aho adharmaḥ sumahān adya me samupasthitaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **vimanā iti diter īpsito’rthas tu indra-maraṇaṁ vinā na sambhaved iti bhāvaḥ ||38||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.39 ||**

**aho arthendriyārāmo yoṣin-mayyeha māyayā |**

**gṛhīta-cetāḥ kṛpaṇaḥ patiṣye narake dhruvam ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.40 ||**

**ko’tikramo’nuvartantyāḥ svabhāvam iha yoṣitaḥ |**

**dhiṅ māṁ batābudhaṁ svārthe yad ahaṁ tv ajitendriyaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **svabhāvam anuvartamānāyā yoṣitaḥ ko’tikramo’parādhaḥ ? ||40||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **atikramo’parādhaḥ | krauryaṁ hi strī-jāteḥ svabhāva eva, tam anuvartantyā anuvartamānāyāḥ ||40||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.41 ||**

**śarat-padmotsavaṁ vaktraṁ vacaś ca śravaṇāmṛtam |**

**hṛdayaṁ kṣura-dhārābhaṁ strīṇāṁ ko veda ceṣṭitam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **svabhāvam evāha dvābhyām | śarat-padmasyevotsavo vikaso yasmin | śravaṇe śrutī, tayor amṛtam | kṣura-dhāropamaṁ cittam ||41||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **svabhāvam evāha—śarad iti ||41||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.42 ||**

**na hi kaścit priyaḥ strīṇām añjasā svāśiṣātmanām |**

**patiṁ putraṁ bhrātaraṁ vā ghnanty arthe ghātayanti ca ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **svāśiṣātmanāṁ svārtha-kāmanayātmavat-preṣṭhatvena pratīyamānānām ||42||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **svasya āśiṣā kāmanayaiva ātmā yatno yāsāṁ, na tu paty-ādi-sukhāpekṣayeti bhāvaḥ | aluk-samāsa āśiṣā śabdaṣ ṭāb-anto vā ||42||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.43 ||**

**pratiśrutaṁ dadāmīti vacas tan na mṛṣā bhavet |**

**vadhaṁ nārhati cendro’pi tatredam upakalpate ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tatredam upakalpate yogyaṁ bhavati | ayaṁ bhāvaḥ—vaiṣṇavaṁ vrataṁ tāvad upadekṣyāmi, tenaivāsyāḥ śuddha-cittāyāḥ indraṁ prati krodho nivartiṣyate | putras tv amartyo bhaviṣyati | dīrgha-kālatve ca vratasya kathañcid vaiguṇye satīndrasya vadho’pi na bhaviṣyatīti ||43||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tatredam upakalpate yogyaṁ bhavati | ayaṁ bhāvaḥ—vaiṣṇavaṁ vrataṁ tāvad upadekṣyāmi, tenaivāsyāś citta-śuddhau satyām indre krodho nivartiṣyate | tataś cendra-vadham anākāṅkṣatyānayā vihitasya vaiṣṇava-vratasya kāmita-duṣphala-dānānarhatvān nendra-ghāṭī bhaviṣyati, kintu vara-prārthanā-pradāna-vākyayor hanti-dhātu-prayogād dhanteś ca gaty-arthatvāt indrānugo’maraḥ putro bhaviṣyati | vratasya dīrgha-kālatve saty avaśyaṁ vaiguṇye ca kiñcid bhaviṣyatīti tenaivāsyā avijñāyā manaḥ samādhānaṁ ca bhaviṣyati | vastutas tu vaiṣṇava-vratasya vaiguṇye’pi phala-siddhir avaśyaṁ bhāvinīty asyāḥ śramaś ca saphala eva bhaviṣyatīti||43||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.44 ||**

**iti sañcintya bhagavān mārīcaḥ kurunandana |**

**uvāca kiñcit kupita ātmānaṁ ca vigarhayan ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.45 ||**

**śrī-kaśyapa uvāca—**

**putras te bhavitā bhadre indra-hā devābāndhavaḥ**[^24]** |**

**saṁvatsaraṁ vratam idaṁ yady añjo dhārayiṣyasi ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **he bhadre, añjaḥ yathāvad yadi dhārayiṣyasi, tarhīndra-hā bhaviṣyati | vaiguṇye tu devābāndhavo bhaviṣyati, vaiṣṇavatvād vratasya | kathañcid vaiguṇye’pi sati sarvathā vaikalyābhāvāt ||45||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **putrasta iti | yadi vrataṁ dhārayiṣyasi, tadā indrahā, tathaiva devānāmasurāṇāṁ ca bāndhavo bhavitā | anyathā tu indrahā na bhavitā, devānām eva bāndhavaśca bhavitetyarthaḥ ||45||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **indrahā indra-ghātī adevānām asurāṇāṁ bāndhava iti ditiṁ bodhayitum iṣṭo’rthaḥ | indrahā indrānugo devānāṁ bāndhava iti svābhīṣṭo’rthaḥ ||45||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.46 ||**

**ditir uvāca—**

**dhārayiṣye vrataṁ brahman brūhi kāryāṇi yāni me |**

**yāni ceha niṣiddhāni na vrataṁ ghnanti yāny uta ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **kāryāṇy āvaśyakāni | vrataṁ yāni na ghnanti, nāvaśyakāni na ca niṣiddhāni kintv abhyanujñātāni | tāni sarvāṇy api brūhi ||46||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.47 ||**

**śrī-kaśyapa uvāca—**

**na hiṁsyād bhūta-jātāni na śapen nānṛtaṁ vadet |**

**na chindyān nakha-romāṇi na spṛśed yad amaṅgalam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **tatraikatriṁśan niṣedhān āha—na hiṁsyād iti pañcabhiḥ | na śapen nākrośet | yad amaṅgalaṁ kapālāsthy-ādikaṁ tan na spṛśet ||47||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **na hiṁsyād iti prathamata evendra-vadhāśaṅkā niṣiddhā ||47||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.48 ||**

**nāpsu snāyān na kupyeta na sambhāṣeta durjanaiḥ |**

**na vasītādhauta-vāsaḥ srajaṁ ca vidhṛtāṁ kvacit ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nāpsu praviśya snāyāt | pūrvaṁ vidhṛtāṁ srajaṁ punar na dhārayet ||48||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **apsu praviśya na snāyāt | adhautaṁ vāso na vasīta, na paridadhyāt | vidhṛtāṁ pūrva-vidhṛtāṁ srajaṁ punar na dhārayet ||48||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.49 ||**

**nocchiṣṭaṁ caṇḍikānnaṁ ca sāmiṣaṁ vṛṣalāhṛtam |**

**bhuñjītodakyayā dṛṣṭaṁ piben nāñjalinā tv apaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **bhojane pañca niṣedhān āha—nocchiṣṭam iti | caṇḍikānnaṁ bhadra-kālyai niveditaṁ pipīlikādi-dūṣitaṁ vā | añjalinā tv apo na pibet ||49||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhojane pañca niṣedhān āha—nocchiṣṭam iti | caṇḍikānnaṁ durgā-niveditam, pipīlikā-spṛṣṭaṁ ca, caṇḍikā syāt pipīlikā ity abhidhānāt | udakyayā rajasvalayā ||49||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.50 ||**

**nocchiṣṭāspṛṣṭa-salilā sandhyāyāṁ mukta-mūrdhajā |**

**anarcitāsaṁyata-vāk nāsaṁvītā bahiś caret ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **gṛhād bahir nirgame sapta niṣedhān āha—nocchiṣṭeti | anarcitā maṇḍana-hīnā | asaṁvītāprāvṛtā ||50||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **gṛhād bahir nirgame sapta niṣedhān āha—nocchiṣṭeti | apṛṣṭa-salilā anācāntā | anarcitā nirbhūṣaṇā | asaṁvītā anāvṛta-sarvāṅgā ||50||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.51 ||**

**nādhauta-pādāprayatā nārdra-pādā udak-śirāḥ |**

**śayīta nāparāṅ nānyair na nagnā na ca sandhyayoḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **śayane’ṣṭau niṣedhān āha—nādhauta-pādeti | nāparāk paścima-śirāḥ ||51||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **aparāṁ paścima-diśamañcati śirasā prāpnoti, aparāṅ tādṛśaṁ yathā syāttatheti kriyā-viśeṣaṇatve’pi tad-viśeṣaṇatva eva tātparyāt, paścima-śirā ityevārthaḥ | yad vā, , aparācī pratīcī | tato lyap-lope pañcamy-antāddik-śabdebhyaḥ [pā. 5.3.27] ity-ādinā svārtha evāstāti-pratyayaḥ | tasya cāñcaterlugiti luk tad-dhita-lugiti strī-pratyayasya luk tato aparāgiti sthite pratīcīmārabhya tāṁ pūrvāṅga-sātkṛtyeti tathaivārthaḥ ||51||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śayane aṣṭau niṣedhān āha—nādhauta-pādeti | aprayatā apavitrā | pavitraḥ parayataḥ pūtaḥ ity amaraḥ | na aparāk paścima-śirāḥ ||51||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.52 ||**

**dhauta-vāsā śucir nityaṁ sarva-maṅgala-saṁyutā |**

**pūjayet prātarāśāt prāg go-viprān śriyam acyutam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **kāryāṇy āha—dhauta-vāsā iti dvābhyām | prātar-āśāt prathama-bhojanāt ||52||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kartavyān āha—prātar-āśāt bhojanāt prāk prātaḥ pūjayet ||52||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.53 ||**

**striyo vīravatīś cārcet srag-gandha-bali-maṇḍanaiḥ |**

**patiṁ cārcyopatiṣṭheta dhyāyet koṣṭha-gataṁ ca tam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **vīra-vatīr jīvad-bhartṛkāḥ | ārcya saṁpūjya | koṣṭha-gataṁ kukṣy-antaragatam ||53||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **vīra-vatīr jīvad-bhartṛkāḥ | koṣṭha-gataṁ kukṣy-antara-gatam ||53||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.54 ||**

**sāṁvatsaraṁ puṁ-savanaṁ vratam etad aviplutam |**

**dhārayiṣyasi cet tubhyaṁ śakra-hā bhavitā sutaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **puṁ-savanaṁ putrotpatti-karam | tubhyaṁ tava ||54||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **puṁ-savanaṁ putrotpatti-karam ||54||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.55 ||**

**bāḍham ity abhyupetyātha ditī rājan mahā-manāḥ |**

**kaśyapād garbham ādhatta vrataṁ cāñjo dadhāra sā ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.56 ||**

**mātṛ-ṣvasur abhiprāyam indra ājñāya mānada |**

**śuśrūṣaṇenāśrama-sthāṁ ditiṁ paryacarat kaviḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mātṛ-ṣvasur diteḥ ||56||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.57 ||**

**nityaṁ vanāt sumanasaḥ phala-mūla-samit-kuśān |**

**patrāṅkura-mṛdo’paś ca kāle kāla upāharat ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.58 ||**

**evaṁ tasyā vrata-sthāyā vrata-cchidraṁ harir nṛpa |**

**prepsuḥ paryacaraj jihmo mṛgaheva mṛgākṛtiḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **harir indro vratasya cchidraṁ prepsuḥ prāptum icchuḥ | jihmaḥ kuṭilaḥ sādhu-veṣaḥ | mṛgahā lubdhako yathā mṛga-vañcanāya mṛga-veṣo bhavati tadvat ||58||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **harir indro vratasya chidraṁ prāptum icchur itīndrasyāpy avijñatvam eva, yato viṣṇoḥ smaraṇena kīrtanena vā sa-cchidram api niśchidraṁ syāt | tasya viṣṇor idaṁ vrataṁ chidre’py acchidram eva bhavet | yad uktaṁ—yasya smṛtyā ca nāmoktyā[^25] [skanda.pu.] iti, mantratas tantrataś chidraṁ [bhā.pu. 8.23.16][^26]ity-ādi ca | kiṁ copariṣṭād indreṇāpi vratasya niśchidratām anubhaviṣyatā vakṣyate—mahāpuruṣa-pūjāyāḥ siddhiḥ kāpy ānuṣaṅgiṇī [bhā.pu. 6.18.74] iti | jihmaḥ kuṭilaḥ | mṛgahā lubdhako mṛga-vañcanāya yathā mṛgākṛtir bhavati, tadvat, tat-paricāraka-lokākṛtiḥ ||58||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.59 ||**

**nādhyagacchad vrata-cchidraṁ tat-paro’tha mahī-pate |**

**cintāṁ tīvrāṁ gataḥ śakraḥ kena me syāc chivaṁ tv iha ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **kena me śivaṁ syād iti cintāṁ prāptaḥ ||59||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.60 ||**

**ekadā sā tu sandhyāyām ucchiṣṭā vrata-karśitā |**

**aspṛṣṭa-vāry adhautāṅghriḥ suṣvāpa vidhi-mohitā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : **aspṛṣṭa-vāriś cāsāv adhautāṅghriś ca ||60||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.61 ||**

**labdhvā tad-antaraṁ śakro nidrāpahṛta-cetasaḥ |**

**diteḥ praviṣṭa udaraṁ yogeśo yoga-māyayā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **nidrayāpahṛtaṁ ceto yasyāḥ ||61||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yogasya para-kāya-praveśākhyasya siddhy-arthā yā māyā, tayā ||61||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.62 ||**

**cakarta saptadhā garbhaṁ vajreṇa kanaka-prabham |**

**rudantaṁ saptadhaikaikaṁ mā rodīr iti tān punaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **mā rodīr ity upalālayann iva tān punaḥ saptadhā cakarta ciccheda ||62||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mā rodīr ity upalālayann iva tān punaḥ saptadhā cakarta ciccheda | atrālpa-kāla eva bahu-puṇya-pāpa-bhojino jīvasya yogino vā kāya-vyūha ivaikakasyaiva jīvasyonapañcāśat kāya-vyāpakatvam iti kecit | bhāvi-dṛṣṭyā prathamam evaikasmin dehe praviṣṭānām ekonapañcāśaj jīvānām indra-kṛta-vibhāgenaikaika-deha-prāptir ity apare | indra-kṛta-khaṇḍeṣv anyeṣām apy aṣṭacatvāriṁśaj jīvānāṁ tat-kṣaṇa eva praveśo yathā latā-gulmānāṁ keṣāñcit khaṇḍa-khaṇḍīkṛtyaiva bhūmāv āropitānāṁ pṛthak pṛthak prarohodgamāt pṛthak pṛthag jīvasya praveśo’numīyate ity ane ca prāhuḥ ||62||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.63 ||**

**tam ūcuḥ pāṭyamānās te sarve prāñjalayo nṛpa |**

**kiṁ na indra jighāṁsasi bhrātaro marutas tava ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **te tam ūcur iti | ata ekasyaiva jīvasya nānā-kāyādhyāsaḥ | yad vā, pūrvam ekasmin dehe bahūnāṁ jīvānām adhyavasthavatāṁ deha-vibhāga-prāpter iti jñeyam ||63||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.64 ||**

**mā bhaiṣṭa bhrātaro mahyaṁ yūyam ity āha kauśikaḥ |**

**ananya-bhāvān pārṣadān ātmano marutāṁ gaṇān ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **kauśika indraḥ | gaṇān sapta | sapta-gaṇā vai marutaḥiti śruteḥ ||64||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mahyaṁ mama | kauśika indraḥ | gaṇān sapta | sapta-gaṇā vai marutaḥiti śruteḥ ||64||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.65 ||**

**na mamāra diter garbhaḥ śrīnivāsānukampayā |**

**bahudhā kuliśa-kṣuṇṇo drauṇy-astreṇa yathā bhavān ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.66-67 ||**

**sakṛd iṣṭvādi-puruṣaṁ puruṣo yāti sāmyatām |**

**saṁvatsaraṁ kiñcid ūnaṁ dityā yad dharir arcitaḥ ||**

**sajūr indreṇa pañcāśad devās te maruto’bhavan |**

**vyapohya mātṛ-doṣaṁ te hariṇā soma-pāḥ kṛtāḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **hariṇā indreṇa śrī-viṣṇuneti vā ||67||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sātmatāṁ puruṣa-samānākāratvaṁ, sajūḥ sahaḥ ||67||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.68-70 ||**

**ditir utthāya dadṛśe kumārān anala-prabhān |**

**indreṇa sahitān devī paryatuṣyad aninditā ||**

**athendram āha tātāham ādityānāṁ bhayāvaham |**

**apatyam icchanty acaraṁ vratam etat suduṣkaram ||**

**ekaḥ saṅkalpitaḥ putraḥ sapta saptābhavan katham |**

**yadi te viditaṁ putra satyaṁ kathaya mā mṛṣā ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.71 ||**

**indra uvāca—**

**amba te’haṁ vyavasitam upadhāryāgato’ntikam |**

**labdhāntaro'cchidaṁ garbham artha-buddhir na dharma-dṛk ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **dityā niṣkapaṭam ukte satīndro’pi niṣkapaṭam evāha—ambeti | labdham antaraṁ yena | arthe eva buddhir yasya ||71||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **dityā niṣkapaṭam ukte satīndro’pi niṣkapaṭam evāha—ambeti | labdhāntaraḥ prāpta-cchidraḥ ||71||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.72 ||**

**kṛtto me saptadhā garbha āsan sapta kumārakāḥ |**

**te’pi caikaikaśo vṛkṇāḥ saptadhā nāpi mamrire ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **me mayā ||72||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.73 ||**

**tatas tat paramāścaryaṁ vīkṣya vyavasitaṁ mayā |**

**mahāpuruṣa-pūjāyāḥ siddhiḥ kāpy ānuṣaṅgiṇī ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **tatastaditi | vyavasitaṁ vicāritam | tad evāha—maheti ||73||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **vyavasitaṁ niścitaṁ tad evāha maheti sārdha-dvayam | kāpi siddhir muktir api ānuṣaṅgikī ||73||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.74 ||**

**ārādhanaṁ bhagavata īhamānā nirāśiṣaḥ |**

**ye tu necchanty api paraṁ te svārtha-kuśalāḥ smṛtāḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : api paraṁ **mokṣam api ||74||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : paraṁ **mokṣam api | **svārtha-kuśalā** iti tena ye tv ārādhanena mokṣam icchanti, te vartamāna-mahā-nidher vinimayena tṛṇārthinaḥ svārthānabhijñāḥ, kintu viṣaya-sādguṇyāt te’pi kṛtārthā evety arthaḥ | yad uktaṁ—satyaṁ diśaty arthitam arthito nṝṇām[^27] [bhā.pu. 5.19.27] iti ||74||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.75 ||**

**ārādhyātma-pradaṁ devaṁ svātmānaṁ jagad-īśvaram |**

**ko vṛṇīta guṇa-sparśaṁ budhaḥ syān narake’pi yat ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **guṇa-sparśaṁ viṣaya-bhogaṁ budhaḥ ko vṛṇīte ? yad yasmān narake’pi viṣaya-bhogaḥ syāt ||75||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **devaṁ krīḍā-param | svātmānaṁ sundara-vigraham ||75||

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.76 ||**

**tad idaṁ mama daurjanyaṁ bāliśasya mahīyasi |**

**kṣantum arhasi mātas tvaṁ diṣṭyā garbho mṛtotthitaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **mahīyasi mahattame | mṛtaḥ sann utthitaḥ ||76||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.18.77-78 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**indras tayābhyanujñātaḥ śuddha-bhāvena tuṣṭayā |**

**marudbhiḥ saha tāṁ natvā jagāma tri-divaṁ prabhuḥ ||**

**evaṁ te sarvam ākhyātaṁ yan māṁ tvaṁ paripṛcchasi |**

**maṅgalaṁ marutāṁ janma kiṁ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi te ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ṣaṣṭhasyāṣṭādaśo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 —o)0(o—


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ ṣaṣṭha-skandhe 


    marud-utpattir nāma 


    aṣṭādaśo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 6.18 ||

(6.19)


### atha ekonaviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ


## puṁsavana-vrata-kathanaṁ

**|| 6.19.1 ||**

**śrī-rājovāca—**

**vrataṁ puṁsavanaṁ brahman bhavatā yad udīritam |**

**tasya veditum icchāmi yena viṣṇuḥ prasīdati ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **

ūnaviṁśe tu yat proktaṁ kaśyapena diter vratam |

tad eva vivṛtaṁ loka-hitāya hari-toṣaṇam ||

tasya prakāram iti śeṣaḥ ||1||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **te tubhyamalaṁ tvad-arthaṁ nānyena prayojanamastītyarthaḥ ||1||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **

viṣṇu-prasādanaṁ cetaḥ kraurya-vidhvaṁsanaṁ vratam | \
nṛpeṇa pṛṣṭo vyavṛṇod ūnaviṁśe muniḥ punaḥ ||

tasya prakāram iti śeṣaḥ ||1||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.2-3 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**śukle mārgaśire pakṣe yoṣid bhartur anujñayā |**

**ārabheta vratam idaṁ sārva-kāmikam āditaḥ ||**

**niśamya marutāṁ janma brāhmaṇān anumantrya ca |**

**snātvā śukla-datī śukle vasītālaṅkṛtāmbare |**

**pūjayet prātar-āśāt prāg bhagavantaṁ śriyā saha ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **mārgaśire māsi śukla-pakṣe | āditaḥ pratipadi ||2|| anumantrya pṛṣṭvā | śuklā dantā yasyāḥ sā śukla-dantī dhauta-dantā | alaṁkṛtā satī pūjayet ||3||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mārgaśire mārgaśīrṣe māsi | āditaḥ pratipadi ||2-3||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.4 ||**

**alaṁ te nirapekṣāya pūrṇa-kāma namo’stu te |**

**mahā-vibhūti-pataye namaḥ sakala-siddhaye ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ādau tāvan namaskāra-mantrān āha tribhiḥ | tubhyam alaṁ paryāptam eva sarvaṁ na kiñcid anyaiḥ kṛtyam asti | ataḥ kevalaṁ te tubhyaṁ namo’stu | paryāptau hetavaḥ—nirapekṣāya, he pūrṇa-kāma mahā-vibhūti-pataye lakṣmī-pataye | sakalāḥ siddhayo’ṇimādyā yasmiṁs tasmai ||4||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : te tubhyam alaṁ t**ā**vad-arthaṁ nānyena prayojanam astīty arthaḥ ||4||**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **alam atiśayena tubhyaṁ nama evāstu | devāntaraṁ yathā nijaiśvarya-siddhy-arthaṁ sevakān apekṣate tathā na tvam ity āha—**nirapekṣāya** svābhāvika-mahaiśvaryavattvād ity arthaḥ | evaṁ **pūrṇa-kāmāyate** kena naivedyādinā prīṇayāmi ? **mahā-vibhūti-pataye** tubhyaṁ | kaiḥ ? gṛhodyāna-gaja-dāsī-nṛtya-gīta-dundubhi-ghoṣa-vādyaiḥ | evaṁ **sakala-siddhaye** svargāpavarga-premādi-siddhi-dātre tubhyaṁ karma-jñāna-yoga-bhakty-ādi-sādhana-gaṇaiḥ kathaṁ prīṇayāmi ? iti bhāvaḥ ||4||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.5 ||**

**yathā tvaṁ kṛpayā bhūtyā tejasā mahimaujasā |**

**juṣṭa īśa guṇaiḥ sarvais tato’si bhagavān prabhuḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **bho īśa ! yathā yathāvat | tvaṁ kṛpādibhir juṣṭaḥ | anyaiś ca satya-saṅkalpatvādibhiḥ sarvair guṇaiḥ | tatas tasmāt ||5||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tad api tvat-kṛpayā sarvaṁ ghaṭata ity āha—**yathā tvaṁ kṛpayā juṣṭaḥ,** tathaiva **bhūty**-ādibhiś ca | **tato** hetos tvam eva **bhagavān asi **ity anvayaḥ | ayam arthaḥ—**kṛpayā** śaktyā **juṣṭaḥ** sevitaḥ san bhakta-datta-tulasī-patra-mātram apy apekṣyamāṇaḥ | "aham adya kṣudhārto'smi kiñcid dehi" iti bhaktāya yācamāno’pūrṇa-kāmo’pi bhavasi, "mama gṛhodyānādikaṁ samprati jīrṇaṁ, kva vilasāmi ?" ity-ādi svapnāntare kurvan vibhūti-śūnyo’pi bhavasi, aṇimādi-siddhi-yukto’pi bhakta-prema-rasanayā baddhaḥ kvāpi gantum api na śaknoṣi | tathaiva bhūtyā mahā-lakṣmyā śaktyā, tejasā sarvānadhīnatayā śaktyā, mahimnā vibhūtyā ca, ojasā balena, sarvair anyaiś ca satya-saṅkalpatvādibhiś ca sarvatra jagati nirapekṣatva-pūrṇa-kāmatvādimāṁś ca bhavasīti, tvam eva bhagavān tvam eva prabhur bhajanīya iti bhāvaḥ ||5||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.6 ||**

**viṣṇu-patni mahā-māye mahā-puruṣa-lakṣaṇe |**

**prīyethā me mahā-bhāge loka-mātar namo’stu te ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **mahā-puruṣasya parameśvarasya lakṣaṇāni nirapekṣatvādīni yasyās tasyāḥ sambodhanam ||6||

krama-sandarbhaḥ : viṣṇu-patnīti | mahā-māye parākhya-śakti-rūpe | ata eva mahā-puruṣa-lakṣaṇe tad-eka-svarūpe ||6||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **itthaṁ bhagavantaṁ praṇamya lakṣmīṁ praṇamed ity āha—viṣṇu-patnīti | mahā-māye māyā-śabdasya śakti-vācitvāt parākhya-śakti-rūpe | ata eva mahā-puruṣasya viṣṇor iva lakṣaṇāni nirapekṣatvādīni yasyāḥ ||6||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.7 ||**

**“oṁ namo bhagavate mahā-puruṣāya **

**mahānubhāvāya mahā-vibhūti-pataye **

**saha mahā-vibhūtibhir balim upaharāmi” iti,**

**anenāhar-ahar mantreṇa viṣṇor āvāhanārghya-pādyopasparśana-**

**snāna-vāsa-upavīta-vibhūṣaṇa-gandha-puṣpa-dhūpa-**

**dīpopahārādy-upacārān susamāhitopāharet.**

**śrīdharaḥ : **pūjā-mantram āha—oṁ nama iti ||7||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **pūjā-mantram āha—oṁ nama iti ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.8 ||**

**haviḥ-śeṣaṁ ca juhuyād anale dvādaśāhutīḥ |**

**oṁ namo bhagavate mahā-puruṣāya mahā-vibhūti-pataye svāheti ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **haviḥ-śeṣam upahārāvaśiṣṭam | homa-mantraṁ darśayati—om iti ||8||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**	**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **haviḥ-śeṣam upahārāvaśiṣṭam ||8||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.9-11 ||**

**śriyaṁ viṣṇuṁ ca varadāv āśiṣāṁ prabhavāv ubhau |**

**bhaktyā sampūjayen nityaṁ yadīcchet sarva-sampadaḥ ||**

**praṇamed daṇḍavad bhūmau bhakti-prahveṇa cetasā |**

**daśa-vāraṁ japen mantraṁ tataḥ stotram udīrayet ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **prakarṣeṇa bhavantyābhyām iti prabhavau ||9-11||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.11-13 ||**

**yuvāṁ tu viśvasya vibhū jagataḥ kāraṇaṁ param |**

**iyaṁ hi prakṛtiḥ sūkṣmā māyā-śaktir duratyayā ||**

**tasyā adhīśvaraḥ sākṣāt tvam eva puruṣaḥ paraḥ |**

**tvaṁ sarva-yajña ijyeyaṁ kriyeyaṁ phala-bhug bhavān ||**

**guṇa-vyaktir iyaṁ devī vyañjako guṇa-bhug bhavān |**

**tvaṁ hi sarva-śarīry ātmā śrīḥ śarīrendriyāśayāḥ |**

**nāma-rūpe bhagavatī pratyayas tvam apāśrayaḥ ||**

**madhvaḥ : **antaryāmī tu yajñāder viṣṇur ijyādinā ramā |


    tat-tac-chabdais tato vācyair na tu sarva-svarūpataḥ ||


    antaryāmī śriyaś cāpi viṣṇur eva na saṁśayaḥ |


    nāntaryāmī kaścid asti viṣṇoḥ kvāpi kutaścana || iti brahma-tarke ||12-13||

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : **ijyā yajñābhinivartakaḥ puruṣa-vyāpāro bhāvanākhyaḥ | kriyā laukikī ||12|| pratyayo nāma-rūpayoḥ prakāśakaḥ | apāśrayas tayor ādhāraḥ ||13||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **yuvām iti sārdhakam | parātparayor api tayor jagat-kāraṇatve hetum āha—iyaṁ hīti | prakṛtir nijāṁśābhāseneti bhāvaḥ ||11||**_tasyā iti | sātvata-tantre—viṣṇos tu trīṇi rūpāṇi ity ādeḥ | tathaivāha—tvam ity-ādi ||12-13||_**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.14 ||**

**yathā yuvāṁ tri-lokasya varadau parameṣṭhinau |**

**tathā ma uttamaśloka santu satyā mahāśiṣaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **parameṣṭhinau parameśvarau ||14||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.15 ||**

**ity abhiṣṭūya varadaṁ śrīnivāsaṁ śriyā saha |**

**tan niḥsāryopaharaṇaṁ dattvācamanam arcayet ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tan niḥsārya mirmālyāpasāraṇaṁ kṛtvā ||15||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.16 ||**

**tataḥ stuvīta stotreṇa bhakti-prahveṇa cetasā |**

**yajñocchiṣṭam avaghrāya punar abhyarcayed dharim ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.17 ||**

**patiṁ ca parayā bhaktyā mahāpuruṣa-cetasā |**

**priyais tais tair upanamet prema-śīlaḥ svayaṁ patiḥ |**

**bibhṛyāt sarva-karmāṇi patnyā uccāvacāni ca ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **mahā-puruṣa-cetasā īśvara-buddhyopanamed bhajet | patiś ca svayaṁ prema-śīlaḥ san patnyāḥ karmāṇi bibhṛyāt, tad-anukūlo bhaved ity arthaḥ ||17||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.18 ||**

**kṛtam ekatareṇāpi dam-patyor ubhayor api |**

**patnyāṁ kuryād anarhāyāṁ patir etat samāhitaḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : **yato dam-patyor madhye ekatareṇa kṛtam ubhayor api bhavati ||18||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.19 ||**

**viṣṇor vratam idaṁ bibhran na vihanyāt kathañcana |**

**viprān striyo vīravatīḥ srag-gandha-bali-maṇḍanaiḥ |**

**arced ahar-ahar bhaktyā devaṁ niyamam āsthitā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **na vihanyān na vicchindyāt ||19||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **na vihanyān na vicchindyāt | agrata iti lyab-lope pañcamī agra-bhāgaṁ yathocitaṁ vibhajyety arthaḥ ||19||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.20 ||**

**udvāsya devaṁ sve dhāmni tan-niveditam agrataḥ |**

**adyād ātma-viśuddhy-arthaṁ sarva-kāma-samṛddhaye**[^28]** ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.21 ||**

**etena pūjā-vidhinā māsān dvādaśa hāyanam |**

**nītvāthoparamet sādhvī kārttike carame’hani ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **dvādaśa-māsān ity ukte kadācit tan-madhye mala-māse sati, tena saha dvādaśa saṅkhyāyāṁ satyāṁ śuddhasyaikasya tyāgaḥ syāt | hāyanam ity ukte tan madhya-patitasya tasyāpi prasaṅgaḥ syāt | tad ubhayaṁ vārayitum ubhayam uktam | upacared upavaset ||21||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **carame’hani paurṇamāsyām ||21||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.22 ||**

**śvo-bhūte’pa upaspṛśya kṛṣṇam abhyarcya pūrvavat |**

**payaḥ-śṛtena juhuyāc caruṇā saha sarpiṣā ||**

**pāka-yajña-vidhānena dvādaśaivāhutīḥ patiḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : **śvo-bhūte prabhāte sati | payasi śṛtena pakvena | pāka-yajña-vidhānena pārvaṇa-sthālī-pāka-vidhānena ||22||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.23 ||**

**āśiṣaḥ śirasādāya dvijaiḥ prītaiḥ samīritāḥ |**

**praṇamya śirasā bhaktyā bhuñjīta tad-anujñayā ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.24 ||**

**ācāryam agrataḥ kṛtvā vāg-yataḥ saha bandhubhiḥ |**

**dadyāt patnyai caroḥ śeṣaṁ suprajāstvaṁ susaubhagam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **suprajāstvaṁ sat-putratvam ity arthaḥ | tad yatas taṁ śeṣam ||24||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : **agrata iti tad-agrima-deśaṁ tyaktvā tad-agre bhojana-niṣedhāt ||24||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śeṣaṁ suprajāstvaṁ suprajastva-karaṁ susaubhaga-karaṁ ca | yad vā, tatas tasya suprajāsvtaṁ syād iti vākyāntaram ||24||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.25 ||**

**etac caritvā vidhivad vrataṁ vibhor**

**abhīpsitārthaṁ labhate pumān iha |**

**strī caitad āsthāya labheta saubhagaṁ**

**śriyaṁ prajāṁ jīva-patiṁ yaśo gṛham ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **jīvatīti jīvaḥ | sa cāsau patiś ceti tam ||25||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.26 ||**

**kanyā ca vindeta samagra-lakṣaṇaṁ**

**patiṁ tv avīrā hata-kilbiṣāṁ gatim |**

**mṛta-prajā jīva-sutā dhaneśvarī**

**sudurbhagā subhagā rūpam agryam ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **avīrā vidhavā | dhaneśvarī saty api yā sudurbhagā sā subhagā bhavati ||26||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **avīrā pati-putra-śūnyā | yā mṛta-prajā sā jīva-sutā dhaneśvarī na bhavati ||26||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.27 ||**

**vinded virūpā virujā vimucyate**

**ya āmayāvīndriya-kalya-deham |**

**etat paṭhann abhyudaye ca karmaṇy**

**ananta-tṛptiḥ pitṛ-devatānām ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **ya āmayāvī rogī sa virujā viśiṣṭayā rujā vimucyate | indriyaiḥ sahitaṁ kalyaṁ dehaṁ ca vindediti śeṣaḥ | paṭhanyo varteta tasya pitṝṇāṁ devatānāṁ cānantā tṛptir bhavatīty arthaḥ ||27||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ya āmayāvī, sa viśiṣṭayā rujā vimucyate | indriyaiḥ sahitaṁ kalyaṁ samarthaṁ dehaṁ ca vindet | abhyudaye ābhyudayika-śrāddhādau ||27||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 6.19.28 ||**

**tuṣṭāḥ prayacchanti samasta-kāmān**

**homāvasāne huta-bhuk śrī-hariś ca |**

**rājan mahan marutāṁ janma puṇyaṁ**

**diter vrataṁ cābhihitaṁ mahat te ||**

**śrīdharaḥ : **upasaṁharati—rājann iti | mahatpuṇyaṁ janma mahadvrataṁ ca ||28||

**krama-sandarbhaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tuṣṭā huta-bhuk śrī-hariś ca ||28||

 —o)0(o—

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ṣaṣṭha ekonaviṁśo’yaṁ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 —o)0(o—


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ ṣaṣṭha-skandhe 

puṁsavana-vrata-kathanaṁ nāma

ekonaviṁśo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 6.19 ||


<!-- Footnotes themselves at the bottom. -->
## Notes

[^1]:
    bhā-sthānīyayā

[^2]:
    tad evaṁ (ya)

[^3]:
    yat 1.2.21-ślokasya sārārtha-darśinyāṁ cakravarti-pādena viśleṣitam, yathā—
    
    satāṁ kṛpā mahat-sevā śraddhā guru-padāśrayaḥ | 
    
    bhajaneṣu spṛhā bhaktir anarthāpagamas tataḥ ||
    
    niṣṭhā rucir athāsaktī ratiḥ premātha darśanam | 
    
    harer mādhuryānubhava ity arthāḥ syuś caturdaśe ||
    tatra prakaraṇe draṣṭavyam |

[^4]:
    _smṛty-ādiṣu_ (BhaktiS MSS : kha,ga,ca)

[^5]:
    The portion between square brackets is not found in all MSS of _Bhakti-sandarbha_ (kha,ga,ca).

[^6]:
    iti saṁstuvatas tasya

[^7]:
    bālakāḥ iti pāṭhāntaraṁ viśvanātha-gṛhītaṁ.

[^8]:
    ity uttareṇānvayaḥ iti paramātma-sandarbha-pāṭhaḥ.

[^9]:
    tat-saṅga-bhraṁśitaiśvaryam iti | jīvasya sva-jñānādi-rūpaṁ darśitam ||15|| iti pāṭhāntaram.

[^10]:
    veginīm iti pāṭhāntaraṁ viśvanāthābhimataṁ.

[^11]:
    _māṁ keśava iti sārdhakam_ | This entire portion is in P only and not in some other editions. 

[^12]:
    kṛt-pratyayāt (ga)

[^13]:
    prābalyaṁ (ṅa), krama-sandarbhe cāyaṁ pāṭhaḥ.

[^14]:
    bhagavat-sandarbha §85.

[^15]:
    bhagavat-sandarbha §19.

[^16]:
    bhagavat-sandarbha §5.

[^17]:
    sakthibhir iti svāmi-pāṭhaḥ.

[^18]:
    nimna-likhitaṁ śloka-catuṣṭayaṁ madhva-sampradāye svīkṛtam—
    
    nānātvaṁ janma-nāśaś ca kṣayo vṛddhiḥ kriyā-phalam |
    
    draṣṭuś ca bhānty atad-dharmā yathāgnerdāhya-vikriyāḥ ||1||
    
    ta ime deha-saṁyogād ātmany ābhānty asad-grahāt |
    
    svapne yathā tathā nānyad dhyāyet sarvaṁ bhayaṁ ca yat ||2||
    
    prasuptasyānahaṁ-mānān na ghorā bhāti saṁsṛtiḥ |
    
    jīvato’pi yathā tadvad vimuktasyānahaṁ-mateḥ ||3||
    
    tasmād anyan mano-mātraṁ jahy ahaṁ-mamatā-tamaḥ |
    
    vāsudeve bhagavati mano dhehy ātmanīśvare ||4||

[^19]:
     deho’savo’kṣā manavo bhūta-mātrā
    nātmānam anyaṁ ca viduḥ paraṁ yat |
    sarvaṁ pumān veda guṇāṁś ca taj-jño
    na veda sarva-jñam anantam īḍe ||

[^20]:
    nānyo’to’sti draṣṭā [bṛ.ā.u. 3.7.23]

[^21]:
    sākṣāt iti hari-bhakti-vilāsa-gītapressayoḥ pāṭhaḥ |

[^22]:
    hari-bhakti-vilāsa-sthita-pāṭhānusāreṇa |

[^23]:
    vidagdhayā

[^24]:
    indra-hādeva-bāndhavaḥ

[^25]:
    _yasya smṛtyā ca nāmoktyā tapo-yajña-kriyādiṣu |_
    nyūnaṁ sampūrṇatāṁ yāti sadyo vande tam acyutam ||

[^26]:
    mantratas tantrataś chidraṁ deśa-kālārha-vastutaḥ |
    sarvaṁ karoti niśchidram anusaṅkīrtanaṁ tava || 
    hari-bhakti-vilāsa 11.376-377 draṣṭavyaḥ.

[^27]:
    satyaṁ diśaty arthitam arthito nṝṇāṁ
    naivārthado yat punar arthitā yataḥ |
    svayaṁ vidhatte bhajatām anicchatām
    icchāpidhānaṁ nija-pāda-pallavam ||

[^28]:
    sarva-kāma-rddhaye tathā.
